## **The Cave King Will Live a Paradise Life - 280 – Two Steps Ahead!?**

---

After separating from Balpas, we returned to the main road. It was filled with carriages and people moving in both directions.

Rienna looked over her shoulder and muttered.

“I thought that someone would follow us.”

“There doesn’t seem to be anyone. After all, he seems like the kind of person who doesn’t like to bother with such troublesome things.”

Fule agreed. Balpas could be rather lazy. And he likely didn’t want to risk offending us by sending out his spies. Also, he seemed to not see us as a threat.

“Well, a lot happened, and so I forgot… But we were supposed to look for a place to stay.”

“That’s right. How about going down the main street? Also, I am curious about the Arubal Company.”

I nodded at Rienna.

“We’ll do that. It would be good to at least see their headquarters.”

And so we made our way through the crowds on the main street.

“I can see it now. Though, it’s still quite far away.”

I turned my eyes towards the spiral tower in the distance. The company flag was blowing in the wind above. And below the tower, there was a large stone building.

“So it is that… While not as high as the World Tree, it is very tall.”

“It’s the tallest tower in the royal capital. Normally, you are not allowed to build anything that is as high as the palace. But they received special permission, as they made great donations to the palace.”

“Huh. So that’s how rich they are…”

Fule looked impressed as she raised her head towards the tower.

Rienna also looked while she walked.

“Still, it seems so far away…as if my sense of distance is all messed up.”

“Because we’re in a crowd. In any case, let’s keep walking.”

We went on for a few more minutes, and then we arrived at the area near the Arubal Company headquarters.

The sturdy building had rows of stone pillars. The first floor was a store, and the front windows had various luxury items on display.

“Oh…this place is so big… Bigger than the others.”

“And there are so many customers.

“Indeed. I can tell how crowded it is inside, by detecting their magic energy.”

Fule squinted her eyes.

“If there were any dangerous devices, we should be able to detect them too…but there doesn’t seem to be anything.”

As Fule said, I did not detect anything powerful from the building.

Rienna said,

“As for lodging, it should also be a place where we can detect magic energy.”

“Indeed. Hmm…?”

There was a well-dressed man standing in front of the company building. He suddenly started to walk towards us.

“Do you have business here? If you are searching for something, maybe I can help you.”

The man was wearing a green coat and a decorated hat. He also wore round glasses with a golden frame.

A merchant. From the Arubal Company.

They must have an employee stationed in the front at all times, ready to speak to passersby.

I answered calmly.

“Well, in a way. I am actually looking for land or a building within the city. And I wondered if there was someone who could help me.”

“I see. Indeed. It so happens that I am in charge of the property handled by the company. If you wish, I could show them to you… Your Highness.”

This was a surprise. Even if they knew about what happened in the Nostor mountains, surely they would not recognize me by sight.

…Had information come from the Lushika store?

“You recognize me?”

“Of course. We also create portraits of the royal family. And as someone in charge of the works of art, I know your face. Besides, we have heard all about your exploits in the Nostor fortress. It is a great honor to meet you.”

“I see…”

“Ah, please forgive me. I have not introduced myself yet. I am Bisto, the president of the Arubal Company.”

So he came to me himself.

Balpas had known about the fortress as well. There had even been a festival in celebration, so it was not strange that the Arubal Company knew about it.

Balpas had said something about how information about Sheorl had leaked to the royals. And the Arubal Company was close with the royal family. And so they likely knew that I was the lord of Sheorl as well.

But I was more interested in the device.

Bisto continued.

“I have visited the Lushika store a few times myself, and so I was worried about Leodor! And it was you who helped us…! Please allow me to act as your guide as a show of gratitude!”

He went out of his way to tell me that he had been to Lushika.

If he knew about the Nostor incident, then he would be interested in the device as well.

According to Alva, it had been Bisto who prepared the teleportation devices.

Nostor mountain. Sheorl. Heal. The combination of things was enough to make me someone they would watch for. 

Bisto seemed to be acting while thinking of the worst case scenario. Perhaps he had decided to act as soon as something strange happened around the Nostor mountains.

And so he made the bold decision to contact me directly.

If so…then perhaps the real culprit had already escaped.

What should I do then…

“Indeed.”

If I left now, they would get suspicious. Also, he probably hadn’t completely lost hope that I hadn’t discovered the device.

“Very well. Please show us some of your properties. Preferably ones with a good view of this street.”

“If that is the case, what about that one over there?”

Bisto pointed at a building on the other side of the street. It was a white, five-story structure. The roof had blue tiles and there were large glass windows. It almost looked like it could be part of the palace.

Not only that, but this was the busiest part of the street. It seemed quite unlikely that such a building would be empty. Though, it appeared that the first floor was being used for storage space and shops.

“It seems to be occupied?”

“Yes. Currently, the lower floor is being used as a warehouse. However, if you wish, you could have the upper floors today, and the lower floors tomorrow.”

“And how much would it cost? In fact, would I be buying it, or paying rent?”

“Whichever you prefer. In fact, we would give it to you for free, Your Highness.”

This was a strange approach. Had he predicted that I had overwhelming power, and decided to try and soften me up?

It was too strange, regardless.

“For free? What do you mean?”

“As I said previously, you saved Lushika, Lord Heal. And you are the king’s son. We would be glad to help you.”

“It is hard to believe. I think you have some other motive.”

Should I bring up the device…?

However, Bisto then replied.

“I have no other motive at all. It is just that those of the royal family have been talking about you a lot recently. And so it is our great wish to become closer to you.”

He did not bring up the device after all.

However, he must want to know.

“I see. Well, I have no intention of getting involved in the power struggles of the palace. I will not be taking any sides.”

“Oh, you misunderstand me. I am but a simple merchant. We wish to be close to you in order to improve our business.”

“Indeed. Well, I was also thinking about trade.”

“Oh! That is wonderful. You should find our company very useful then.”

“I will consider it. Now, about those properties?”

“Certainly. Right away!”

Bisto then called some boys who were close by.

“Contact the store. All work must be halted. I am going to guide some customers.”

“Yes, Sir Bisto!”

The boys ran off towards the store.

“Now, please follow me.”

Bisto started to walk, and so we followed after him.

On the way, Bisto continued to talk.

“Still, I was very surprised to hear about that business in the Nostor mountains. How did you manage to take that fortress?”

Here it comes. He really did want to know about that device.

“Sorry, but it’s a military secret.”

“I apologize for asking.”

Bisto withdrew immediately. And so I tried being more aggressive.

“However…we did acquire a lot of loot.”

“Oh…? How wonderful. What kind of loot?”

His voice changed very subtly. He probably thought the device was among the loot.

“They had a lot of weapons and armor that were too valuable for bandits to own. And their foot supplies and other luxury items were also impressive. I made quite a profit on them.”

“That is good to hear. Still, I heard that the mountains are a severe place. How did they manage to store so much in that fortress?”

Of course, he knew the answer already. But anyone who did not would definitely wonder about it.

“I was curious about that as well. But the bandits all told me that only their captain knew the answer to that. And this captain…he ended up taking his own life. What was his name? Oh, that’s right. It was Berido.”

In fact, he attempted to. But we stopped him. However, this news would surely put Bisto’s mind at ease.

“Is that so? While I cannot say it too loudly, there must be a lot of secret things going on between the different lords.”

He was suggesting it was one of the other lords of neighboring territories who did it. Well, it was the most obvious explanation. 

“I don’t care about that right now. I only acted because such bandits should not be allowed to continue committing such crimes.”

“It was an honorable deed.”

Just then, a voice rang from behind.

“Huh, mister. You defeated some bandits.”

“Amazing!”

When I turned around, I saw some girls and boys holding documents. They were well-dressed, but had a roughness about them too. They must be working for Bisto.

Bisto turned around and raised his voice.

“All of you! Hold your tongues!”

“I’m sorry, Sir Bisto! I just came to deliver the report from the northern branch. But you were busy….”

“That can wait… No, I did tell you to bring it at once. I’ll look into it later. Go home for today.”

Bisto gave them a copper coin and sent them away.

“Thank you, Sir Bisto!”

“Please hire us again!”

“Hmm.”

Bisto smiled and waved his hand. Then he turned around and bowed to me.

“I beg your pardon, Lord Heal.”

“No, it’s fine. I had heard that you give work to orphaned or poor children. So it was true.”

“One does not like to hoard wealth… Besides, I am an orphan myself.”

“Indeed? That is very commendable.”

“I am honored that you think so.”

He really did not seem like a villain…

After that, Bisto started to show us the property.

The property was introduced in a very straightforward manner, covering things like layout, the age of the building, and how comfortable it would be during each season. He did not bring up the device. Perhaps he really was relieved after hearing of Berido’s death.

While I wasn’t sure at first, I ended up just buying the property. There was nothing suspicious about it, and it was close enough to keep an eye on the Arubal Company.

At first, he insisted that it should be given to us for free, but I sternly asked if he was mocking me, and so he finally agreed to sell it.

And like that, we succeeded in securing lodging and making contact with Bisto.

++++

# **Pupil of the Wiseman - Chapter 322 - Adams Residence**

Since Alma was the empress of the entire country, and Esmeralda commanded the whole army, there were no files off-limits to them, allowing them to see all the information recorded in the archives.

“Now that’s what I call an upstanding man.”

That also included all of Adams’ past exploits.

His full name was Henry Adams. He was currently the commander of a knight unit, and had an excellent track record throughout his career.

He had graduated from the top knight academy in Nirvana as one of their best students. Then when he joined the forces, he ended second place in a swordsmanship tournament, and his team emerged winner in a group jousting tournament. He had earned many other awards as well, demonstrating his valor and courage. He was more than fit to lead his unit of knights.

“Oh wait, this is the knight Augusto told us about.”

Esmeralday suddenly brought that up.

With how big Nirvana was, they required three different armies, each of which had four knight orders, and each order had thirty two units of knights.

Henry was part of the 16th knight unit, the heavy armored land troops. Their previous commander was someone called Augusto, who had also been part of Esmeralda’s own troops.

Now Henry Adams had taken Augusto’s place as commander.

“Ah, I see, now I remember his father. So he’s from that Adams family…”

As they went through the files, Alma recalled something. Henry Adams was the son of a knight who had been serving her around twenty five years ago as well.

Alma had been in this world for five years by then, and Lloyd Adams, the father of Henry Adams, had been a great help to her when fending off monsters, which was her main priority at the time.

Seeing that his talents had also been passed on to his son brought a smile to Alma.

It also made sense that the woman from earlier had caught feelings for him. Also, as the Spirit King would tell Mira later, Martel had secretly been really excited about it all and it had been tricky to keep her under control.

The three began to get more excited to meet Henry Adams, now that they knew a bit more about what kind of person he was. He arrived around two minutes after they were done looking up information about him.

“Did you call for me, Empress Alma, Lady Esmeralda? I’m Henry Adams, at your service.”

There was a knock on the door before that voice rang from the other side, sounding rather nervous. But that was not his fault, as anyone would be nervous after being summoned by those two.

“Please come in, thank you for coming.”

Once Esmeralda told him to enter the room, the door opened and he passed through politely.

“What did you need me for? I’ll do anything you request.”

He knelt elegantly in front of Alma, his manners still impeccable despite his unease for being summoned out of the blue like that. He really was an excellent knight, just like his records said.

But Mira was rather surprised seeing him for the first time.

She had seen how enamored the woman was with him, and he came from a family of knights, inheriting the talents of his father and becoming the commander of a unit.

All of that seemed like the stereotypical traits of a knight, so in her mind, she also imagined him looking like the classic knight, with a dashing appearance that stole the hearts of all women around him.

Now that he was there, she realized that Henry was quite different from everything she had imagined.

As he was kneeling, his head was still level with Mira’s. He was a giant more than two meters tall, with powerful bulging muscles, which made him look like he could swing an enormous greatsword effortlessly with just one arm.

He also lacked the handsome face Mira thought all knights had. Instead, he appeared more like a pirate or a mercenary that had changed his ways. He was far more masculine, and the best way to describe him was that he was like a bear.

(Now even I want to cheer them on!)

Now that Mira knew he looked the opposite of what she had imagined, and that he was not the type of hot guy all girls gushed over, she also became invested in Henry and the woman from earlier’s love story, though not to the same extent as Martel.

“Actually we just want to ask something…”

Mira began asking about Meimei who was staying at the Adams residence, while thinking rather rudely that the woman had to have fallen in love with his personality, as there was no way his appearance could cause that.

---

“It really is really big…”

Around one hour after they met Henry, Mira arrived at the Adams residence. The Adams lineage as knights was still young, but their mansion was already a sight to behold. Past the large front gates came a neatly kept garden, and with the main building standing tall further in.

“Please follow me, she’s probably still with my siblings right around this time.”

Henry was showing her around the mansion, as he explained that he also had two brothers and two sisters who were far younger than him.

All four of them were always getting into trouble, but he did not seem upset as he talked about it.

Back at the palace, they had told Adams how they were looking for someone, and that the girl he had invited to his home, Meimei, could be her. When they described Meilin to him, he agreed that everything matched perfectly as well.

That was enough to convince Alma that it had to be Meilin, and so she instructed Henry to take Mira to his house to meet Meimei.

“Oh, so she’s been babysitting? That’s a bit hard to imagine…”

Mira grimaced a little at the thought of Meilin, someone who usually spoke with her fists, watching over children. That was such a disconnect that she even began to dread it was actually a different person.

But her doubts would clear up soon enough, as Mira followed Henry further into the residence.

“Yes, it seems they’re still going at it.”

They reached a door, with violent noises audible on the other side, as well as various vigorous shouts and the shaking of things colliding. Mira began to wonder what kind of babysitting would lead to such noises, and Henry opened the door.

“Ohhh, now I get it. I should’ve expected this from a family of knights.”

A warm breeze escaped from the room when the door opened, and the noises became louder. And what Mira saw inside placated all her questions.

Meimei and Henry’s siblings had been in the mansion’s training area. So in other words, rather than babysitting, Meimei had been training them for battle.

(Hmm…I don’t recognize her clothes, but those movements…yes, that’s definitely Meilin!)

The floor was made of stones set in place with earth, and the walls and ceiling were made of stone. One of the walls was also almost entirely occupied by a window, offering a panoramic view of the garden, which was wide open to let a refreshing breeze into the room.

Somehow the training room felt more spacious inside than it did outside, and there were five children there.

One of them, who appeared to be the oldest, wearing an outfit that was reminiscent of a chinese dress, with a face that appeared naive and innocent, but with a clearly well toned body, was Meilin.

From the look of things, they were fighting one against four, but with Meilin’s advantage in strength and experience, she was able to easily fend off the children’s wooden swords with her bare hands. But the children would not give up, constantly standing back up as their desire to grow stronger was set ablaze.

Mira and Henry also recognized that motivation, so they watched from a distance to not interfere.

Around five minutes passed like that.

“Ah, it’s Henry!”

“Henryyy!”

After being thrown to the ground by Meilin, a young boy and girl caught sight of Henry.

“Ah, you’re right!”

“Welcome back.”

Hearing that, the other two children also turned around, and broke into bright smiles as they began to run up to their older brother.

But before they could get too far, their small bodies were flung into the air. Meilin had rushed up to them so fast that she could not be seen, mercilessly and ruthlessly throwing the pair.

“Carelessness is the biggest enemy. Never turn your back to an enemy.”

Meilin sharply reprimanded the two as they rolled on the ground, and once they stopped, they jumped on their feet and replied energetically. It was clear that they held Meilin and her teachings in high esteem.

Meanwhile, Mira grimaced a little, seeing that Meilin was still as unforgiving as always.

When they realized Henry was there, the children took a break from training as they rushed up to him, this time without being struck from behind.

“Let me introduce them. This is the oldest of the bunch Ryan, and our younger brother Fabian. And this is the older sister Cinthia and the younger Rosemary.”

Henry plopped his hand down on the heads of the children as he introduced each one of them, who reacted either by standing proud or looking embarrassed when it was their turn. And out of all of them, Ryan’s reaction was the strongest.

His face was reddening, almost like he had forgotten how to breathe as he tried to stand tall and confident. That was the moment when that boy who aspired to be a knight fell in love for the first time.

“So bro- Henry, who…who is she?”

Ryan’s voice quivered with nervousness as he asked that, and Henry replied with a quick nod before introducing Mira to them.

“She is Mira, an experienced adventurer according to Lady Esmeralda. And she was looking for Meimei, so I brought her to visit. Please treat her with respect.”

Hearing that, the children’s reactions visibly changed. For a moment, they looked at her with far more serious and reverent eyes, but a moment later that was completely overshadowed by infantile curiosity again.

“An adventurer? That’s so cool!”

“Are you strong? What Rank do you have?!”

No matter in what country or in what city, adventurers were always popular. There was something about their brazenly straightforward and unique way of life that especially made children adore them. It did not matter if they were children of a family of knights, they still were just as impressed by adventurers.

But Ryan’s mind was clouded by a mix of emotions, as he held both admiration and a budding love. There was nothing more painful than realizing the girl of one’s dreams was standing far out of reach for him.

“Ohh, you want to know?”

Mira basked in the admiration and curiosity of the children, standing arrogantly before replying, already dreaming of the reaction they would give once she told them she had reached Rank A already.

But someone would interrupt her before that would happen.

“You, I already know who you actually are.”

Meilin, who had been silently staring at Mira the whole time, suddenly raised her voice declaring that.

The worst possibility flashed in Mira’s mind.

Being so well-versed in martial arts, Meilin had the special ability of detecting even the most minuscule movements on others, allowing her to identify people by their mannerisms or footsteps. Now Mira was dreading the possibility that Meilin had noticed some inconspicuous habit of hers that would tie her to Danbulf, and was about to announce it to everyone present.

“Wait, stop, don’t—!”

Since Meilin likely did not know anything yet, she would likely not hesitate to reveal the truth, pushing Mira to attempt to silence her. But that was of no use, as Meilin’s confident voice was far louder.

“You are definitely the Spirit Queen!”

After Meilin’s announcement, the children quickly became riled up. Mira was not just an experienced adventurer, but one so renowned she had her own nickname.

Meilin had the strange ability to quickly learn about powerful people, so she was also quite familiar with the Spirit Queen. And now that she had revealed that, the children were even more excited.

(Oh, she went there.)

In contrast to that, Mira had never felt more relieved. While Meilin had ruined her big reveal for the children, she had managed to keep her true identity secret.

Even Meilin’s discerning eye was not able to see through Mira’s current appearance, and would not notice that unless Mira moved around a bit more.

“Humm… So you’ve seen through my disguise. But yes, you’re correct, I’m none other than the Spirit Queen!”

Mira puffed her chest in an exaggerated manner, seeing how excited the children were and Meilin’s high expectations that her guess was correct. As soon as she did that, the children’s faces lit up with joy.

“Woahh, that’s incredible!”

“She’s a queen!”

There was a mix of surprise and admiration in their eyes, which also pleased Mira as she smiled back saying, “Mhm, I’m so amazing.”

But there was someone there who was smiling even more intensely than the children and Mira…it was Meilin.

“Yes, just like I thought! We were doomed to meet like this!”

Those were the words that came out of Meilin’s mouth, even though she seemed overjoyed. But Mira just let out a sigh while shaking her head, not even questioning whether she had done something for Meilin to have a bad opinion of her.

“I don’t think that means what you think it does…”

This was something that frequently happened with Meilin, which brought back a lot of memories to Mira as she pointed that out. Meilin tilted her head in confusion for a moment, before asking, “Oh right, then you came just like a moth flying to the fire?”

“That’s not quite it either.”

Mira chuckled awkwardly hearing that, and Meilin frowned as she tried to think about it more. That only lasted for a few seconds before she gave up and just said, “Well, who cares!” before rushing up to Mira and adding, “Please fight me!”

(Obviously it came to this.)

That was something she had already anticipated.

Meilin was constantly on the move, wandering through the continent in search of stronger rivals, so it was natural for her to also see an adventurer that was growing in popularity as someone she wanted to fight. Especially someone who came out of nowhere like the Spirit Queen.

(Either way, I should focus on my mission first.)

Mira had been looking for Meilin with a specific goal in mind. To aid her in concealing her identity as one of the Nine Wisemen before she participated in the tournament.

If they began fighting here, it would lead to a violent brawl between two Wisemen. That would become an explosive event that would stand out a lot, and if they stood out, the chances of people recognizing them would increase, especially before Mira could give Meilin her disguise.

“Very well, I’ll take you up on that!”

But before Mira realized, those words escaped her mouth.

That was because there was no better candidate than Meilin to test out everything she had theorized during her experiments before, as she was essentially on the same level as Mira.

There was also the reaction she noticed in the children when Meilin made the request. It was clear they were excited to see who was stronger, their teacher Meimei or the Spirit Queen.

If she declined the match, it would look like a summoner was weak and running away, and Mira would never allow that to happen.

“Yes! Thank you thank you!”

Meilin jumped in happiness, and then quickly got ready, taking a wide stance with one hand high and the other low, ready to counter any attack, and said, “Summon all you want.”

But Mira shook her head.

“You don’t have to be considerate. A true summoner can adapt to any situation in battle.”

Being able to summon anything she wanted beforehand would give her too much of an advantage in a one versus one match, so Mira declared there was no need for such a handicap, and instead grinned as she said, “Or rather, you’ll have to act soon if you don’t want to get crushed.”

Mira was very familiar with Meilin’s fighting style. She loved to fight, so she was always on the offensive. The only time she would take a defensive stance was to gauge her opponent’s strength at the start of a fight, so she could limit her own strength to match it. That was her favorite way of fighting new opponents and improving her own skills.

That was why Mira also readied herself and warned her. If Mira got a headstart, she would defeat Meilin in an instant.

“Ah, I think you’re right.”

Seeing Mira’s stance, and more importantly, the resolute aura around her, Meilin understood that Mira was different from all the previous opponents she had encountered. That made her smile as she lowered her body to increase the amount of explosive speed she could unleash, which she was so adept at.

“You give the signal.”

Meilin said that, as she and Mira both looked at Henry. He instantly knew what they wanted from him, as he was also a trained fighter, and walked over to stand just in the middle between Mira and Meilin.

“Ready… Fight!”

Henry raised his hand, and the instant he swung it down, Mira and Meilin’s intense fight began.

+++

# **323: Mira vs. Meilin**

Mira had been looking for Meilin, another of the Nine Wisemen. Her search led her to the Nirvana Empire, where her efforts and the help of Empress Alma led her to meet the knight Henry Adams, at whose home Meilin had been staying.

Now reunited, they went right ahead to start a match in the Adams Residence’s training grounds.

“Let’s go!”

As soon as Henry gave the signal to start, Meilin’s delightful smile turned into a ferocious look like a predator stalking its prey, and she vanished.

Henry and his siblings watched with their mouths open, but Mira remained calm as she scouted her surroundings to find her.

(It’s just like I expected.)

While it appeared like Meilin had vanished, in reality she had just used an ability of Sages, Ground Shrink. Mira used it quite frequently as well, so she was familiar with how it worked.

It allowed the user to move blindingly fast while ignoring all laws of inertia, but that came with some limitations.

First was that one could only move in a straight line, second was that once activated, it could not be stopped. In other words, it made it impossible to dodge an attack if one’s opponent anticipated where Ground Shrink would end.

Knowing Meilin, she would most likely use Ground Shrink for a full on frontal attack, so Mira focused most of her attention in front of her, but her trained ears would not let her miss anything either.

“There!”

The sound she heard was slightly louder to the left behind her, and she recognized it as the particular sound effect of entering and leaving Ground Shrink, even if it was barely audible since Meilin had been using that ability for far longer, and she only needed an instant to recover and weave in her next action.

Still, it was enough of an audio clue for Mira to act in response, immediately partially summoning a tall tower shield between her and the noise.

Mira also knew that Meilin liked to use Ground Shrink as a feint before using it again to attack from much closer, as she could be far more shrewd and underhanded than her appearance would suggest. After all, it would be impossible for someone to reach her level if they were easy to read and see through.

But as Mira had known Meilin for so long, she knew about that possibility.

That shield appeared in the path between them with the perfect timing to block Meilin’s advance with Ground Shrink, guaranteeing a collision.

“Too easy!”

Instead of stopping her, the shield shattered.

Meilin had chosen to attack and break through the shield with a powerful knee strike coupled with the speed of Ground Shrink. That shield was strong enough to withstand attacks from powerful magic beasts, but it was easy work for Meilin.

“How…!”

Mira quickly jumped back while leaving behind a bunch of Dark Knights surrounding Meilin. That only bought Mira a little time, as Meilin kicked off the ground to propel herself into the air, kicking away one of the Dark Knights and using the recoil to turn around and barely evade the sword of another Dark Knight, after which she continued spinning around and taking them down.

(She’s definitely grown stronger since I last saw her…)

As far as Mira knew, there was only a limited number of moves that could be pulled right after Ground Shrink, one of which were knee strikes. Still, Meilin’s movements were clearly swifter and more precise than in the game days, showing how much she had improved with all her training since then.

It was not just the shield either, Dark Knights also fell in one strike when confronting her. That shocked Mira, but she was used to being impressed by Meilin like that, so she was not phased as she quickly thought of her next move.

“Then what about this?”

Before Meilin was done spinning around and could amend her stance, Mira took her next move, this time surrounding her with six Ashen Knights. Meilin was not the only one who had grown stronger.

“I’ve never seen these before!”

Ashen Knights were still Armor Spirits, but they were clearly different from the common Dark and Holy Knights. Seeing their refined and more powerful appearance was a surprise to her, but it also brought a smile to her face, as she clearly was enjoying it.

That did not slow down Meilin in the least, as she continued chaining moves like flowing water. All of the Ashen Knights began by utilizing simultaneous shield strikes, not allowing Meilin to move aside, but she found a way out by jumping up and above them.

“Then how about this!”

Meilin was moving like a wild animal evading everything, but Mira had already anticipated that escape, and accordingly began using Sage Arts of her own, specifically Refined Impact that sent focused shockwaves at Meilin.

“That’s not enough!”

A moment later, there was a thunderous noise as all the Ashen Knights were flung into the air, with one of them flying to the specific spot to block the line of sight between Mira and Meilin.

(So she’s finally grasping.)

That was the ability that had coined her nickname of Grasping Meilin. Its true name was Unhanded Dream, which could expand her physical reach into the confines of her perception.

In practice, that meant she was able to _grasp_ anything even if it was far away, allowing her to turn a variety of Sage Arts that usually required direct touch like grappling moves into ranged attacks.

She had combined that with Furious Grasp, a powerful Sage Art that produced a destructive shockwave that sent enemies flying and crushed them.

Meilin used that to lift the Ashen Knights into the air and block Mira’s Refined Impact, which caused a powerful tremor that shook the whole training area.

All of that had opened a hole on the ceiling, and as the Ashen Knights made clanking sounds while falling down, Mira realized Meilin was no longer there.

But Mira’s ears would not miss that faint noise, indicating Ground Shrink was being used nearby.

“Head on this time!”

Mira realized Meilin was going to be landing right in front of her, so she instinctively jumped back.

An instant later, Meilin’s jumping kick passed through there. Mira would have been in really bad shape if she had not dodged.

“So you dodged again!”

Meilin’s voice was filled with joy as she flew through the air, quickly using Sky Stride to change directions and rush at Mira again.

“Woah?!”

Meilin’s swift attack forced Mira to twist her body back to dodge again, but that was only the beginning of her next troubles.

All of Meilin’s actions had been skillfully chosen to force Mira into a close range fight, something Mira felt rather comfortable with, except that all her knowledge had been passed onto her from none other than Meilin herself. There was still a rift in skill between master and pupil, so there was no chance Mira could win like that.

The only thing keeping the match going were the Holy Knights being summoned one after another endlessly, and the multitude of partial summonings Mira used.

“They just keep coming!”

As Meilin swiftly punched and kicked the Holy Knights away, she looked thoroughly entertained, as it had been a long time since she had met an opponent that allowed her to unleash so much of her power.

The many Holy Knights served to keep Meilin away, and some others to thwart her attacks. Despite their strong defenses, they all broke after a few hits from Meilin, but that was enough to keep her at bay.

And even when she got dangerously close, Mira would use partial summoning to instantly defend herself.

Still, Mira was aware that she could not continue like that. Meilin was gradually growing used to the Holy Knights and partial summoning, so her speed was increasing.

“To think they would become less useful this quickly…”

Mira tried to switch things around partially summoning spears, battleaxes, bows, and so on, an ability Mira herself had only discovered recently, but Meilin adapted to it quickly.

And then the critical moment came. Meilin tore through a Holy Knight, stepping in mid-air for a follow-up flying kick to shatter the partially summoned shield covering Mira.

Mira barely avoided the kick using Mirage Step, but she was not out of danger yet, as Meilin quickly turned around and threw an explosive punch straight at Mira.

A direct hit from that punch would at best leave Mira unconscious, but Meilin had calculated that she could use that amount of power through their fight so far. If Mira blocked the hit with her arms, she would merely be rendered unable to continue fighting.

“Still as speedy as always, I see.”

Meilin’s ability to rapidly chain one attack after another with so much precision was always impressive, and if this had been Mira’s first time seeing it, the match would already be over. Luckily Mira was very familiar with it, and knew how to deal with it, so she was almost baiting Meilin to do it.

Mira crossed her arms to defend herself, and secretly do something more.

She deployed her Holy Knight Frame at just the right moment. That was Mira’s way of compensating for her inferior physical strength, and came in handy just in situations like her current one. It also allowed her to distort Meilin’s perfect control over her strength, giving her a slight edge.

It felt like a heavy impact passed through all of Mira’s body as she completely stopped the attack and then took hold of Meilin’s hand.

“Oh, you managed to stop that?!”

Meilin’s eyes were twinkling like she was expecting even more from this fight, while also looking surprised that her attack had been blocked like that.

“Summoners can do this too!”

Mira shouted loudly, announcing the new possibility for summoners she had discovered, while maintaining her grip on Meilin’s arm, swinging her around before throwing her away with all her strength.

Usually, Mira’s strength would not be enough to do much when throwing someone like that, but now she was aided by her Holy Knight Frame. It not only improved her defenses, but also gave her the same strength of a Holy Knight.

As a result, Meilin flew in a straight line after Mira swung her around, crashing wildly into the wall.

A loud booming sound shook the room while the bulletin board hung on the wall shattered to pieces. No regular person would be able to survive something like that unscathed, and Henry with his siblings watched in shock, wondering if Meilin was alright.

But then…

“I wasn’t expecting that!”

They all heard Meilin’s joyful voice, and the dust settled to reveal her completely safe, her feet planted on the wall, having absorbed the impact like a pair of springs.

“I know, I know.”

Meanwhile, Mira did not seem at all surprised that Meilin had not taken any damage, and merely laughed boastfully. She had been fully confident that Meilin would not take any damage from something like that.

But what happened next did surprise Mira.

“Let’s bring things up a notch!”

Meilin was thrilled to continue the fight as she straightened her legs, and then began walking on the wall. She went up to the ceiling, and even began walking upside down, almost like gravity had no power over her. Henry and his siblings were also shocked by all that.

“That’s a nifty trick you have there.”

That also reminded Mira that she had seen that before. Sasori, one of the Fifty Bells’ Hidden, had also done something similar before.

She had explained that it was a secret ability passed down in her hometown, the Karasawa Village hidden in the western Grimdart forest, but if an outsider managed to impress the elder with their talents, they were also allowed to learn it. That was likely how Meilin acquired it.

“By the way, could you teach me how to do that too?”

Mira was already planning on visiting Karasawa Village to learn that, but just in case she decided to ask that.

“I can’t do that. I promised not to teach anyone.”

Hearing that, Mira was certain that it was the same ability Sasori had used. Meilin’s talents would have impressed anyone too, so it stood to reason that they had allowed her to learn it, as she effortlessly kept walking upside down.

“And you promised that to the elder of Karasawa Village?”

“Yes.”

Meilin replied with a hint of pride in her voice. She treated that ability with respect, knowing how secretive the village was about it.

The elder had likely tested her ability to keep secrets on top of her talent before teaching her. And as naive as she usually seemed, Meilin was surprisingly inflexible when it came to promises, so Mira would not be able to learn it from her.

But then Meilin said something else, “But if you defeat me, I might think about it,” with her eyes set ablaze.

“Oh, I hope you remember that later then.”

Thanks to their long friendship, Mira knew exactly what Meilin was attempting to do, saying that when she had promised to keep silent.

First, she was trying to get Mira to fight even more relentlessly with the idea of such a reward, while also being fully confident that she would not be defeated.

Still, she had only agreed to _think_ about it, not actually do it, as a failsafe in case something unexpected happened. Usually in such cases, she would say she thought about it, and the answer was no. A rather underhanded escape.

That was a piece of wisdom imparted on them by Solomon. Even the Nine Wisemen were not undefeatable, and could meet their match when they least expected it.

Meilin was no exception, and she had already leaked various secrets and tactics after getting carried away with her wagers during fights. So Solomon had to step in and taught her to always say, “I’ll think about it if you win.”

Meilin happily agreed to do that, as long as it meant that her opponents would fight earnestly while keeping herself honest. That habit continued even now.

That also meant that Mira already knew what would happen if she won, and despite that, Mira still agreed on it simply because she too wanted an all out fight.

There was a moment of silence as both opponents stared at each other.

The children had almost forgotten how to breathe as they watched in anticipation, wondering what they would do next. Henry was also rather excited to witness a fight between two highly skilled opponents, so much so he did not seem to notice the crumbling walls around him…

Meilin was the first one to move, running on the ceiling for a moment before vanishing with Ground Shrink.

Then Mira reacted, turning around and holding her arms crossed in front of her face to block Meilin’s incoming flying kick.

And that was when things started to differ from their earlier fight. Right after the block, a black arm swinging a sword appeared, but Meilin vanished before it connected.

She reappeared behind Mira, punching her back, the impact of which was felt strongly by Mira.

“Hnghh…!”

Mira quickly turned around to strike back, only to find Meilin had already vanished again, this time reappearing from the side to attack Mira again, who reacted almost instantly, but to no avail.

(I still can’t compete in these situations…)

A close range fight against Meilin was one of the worst matchups for Mira, especially in an enclosed space, as she could use the walls and ceiling as additional footholds, allowing her to freely move in all three dimensions.

The only reason why the fight had not ended yet was because of Mira’s Holy Knight Frame. Wearing a summon as armor was clearly the superior option to any regular armor.

It not only increased Mira’s defenses greatly, but she could apply the same type of barriers to it as to any summon, allowing her to fully negate a large chunk of damage.

In other words, if she managed it correctly, she could fight as recklessly as she wanted without getting hurt.

“I didn’t think that armor was going to be so tough.”

Meilin looked curiously at Mira, who stood up unscathed after being kicked away for the umpteenth time. She had been trying to measure the strength of Mira’s Holy Knight Frame, attacking from various blind spots and with strikes of varying power.

“This is one of my most recent favorites. You won’t be able to break through it so easily.”

Mira said as she stood up unbothered, fully aware that without armor, she would have been knocked out ten times over. Then again, she could hardly track Meilin’s movements with her eyes, and as Meilin gradually sped up, even reacting to sound cues was getting nearly impossible.

All her five senses could only react the instant before she was hit, so she had to rely on Life Sensing to find Meilin’s position and brace each time.

Regardless of how sturdy it was, the Holy Knight Frame had already endured countless hits and it was only a matter of time before it would break. And Mira had not been sitting idle waiting for that to happen. Her eyes had been constantly darting all around the training area, despite how impossible it was to follow Meilin’s movements, and it was about to pay off.

“Let’s see how you like my other recent favorite then!”

Mira grinned at the chance to put her experiments to use, as a multitude of magic circles appeared all over the training area.

“Ohh, I can feel a lot of mana!”

Meilin appeared slightly wary of that, but in reality was really curious and did not want to miss whatever Mira would do. In a corner of the room were Henry and his siblings too, filled with a multitude of feelings as they continued to watch.

“Oh, it’s just the same as before.”

Meilin appeared slightly let down after having watched with such high expectations.

All the magic circles produced were dozens of Holy Knights, which Meilin had already defeated multiple times in the fight. The only difference seemed to be their number, as the whole training area was crowded by them now.

“Oh, just keep watching.”

Mira just grinned even more, finally activating the gimmick as she turned all her summons into Holy Lords.

Their shields became taller and wide like walls, which the Holy Lords held with both hands to create an enhanced defense that would resist Meilin’s attacks much better.

On top of that, their sheer number made the training area feel even more congested. Even if Meilin continued using the walls and ceiling to move around, there were too many obstacles for her to gain much speed. So she would need to deal with the Holy Lords first before being able to unleash her full power again.

And Mira’s plan did not end there. Thanks to her connection to the Spirit King, she had also imbued the Holy Lords with the power of a Light Spirit, giving them a blinding shine.

As a result, the whole training area turned so bright it was impossible to see anything.

“This is too bright!”

Meilin closed her eyes, overwhelmed by the bright light, and Mira laughed haughtily while also closing her eyes.

“Is that also something summoners can do? That’s an interesting power.”

“I can’t see anything Henryyy.”

Henry and his siblings were also blinded by the light, which felt like looking straight at the sun. But that also meant that no one would be able to see how the summons would fight after that.

“Let’s see how you fight in this situation.”

Neither of the opponents could see the other, but Mira knew where Meilin was with Life Sensing. Then again, that was a Sage Art so Meilin could use it as well. But that did not even the field fully.

As the summoner, Mira knew the exact position of every single Holy Lord, while Meilin did not.

“This is annoying.”

Mira walked freely through the blinding light, and whenever Meilin tried to move closer, she would be stopped by the Holy Lords, which used their massive shields to strike her.

Meilin was still able to barely dodge those attacks by their presence and noise, but Mira had also thought a step further, selecting a few of the dozens of Holy Lords to be stealthy ones with the power of a Spirit of Stillness.

It did not take long for Meilin to wander too close to one of those and be struck by a shield bash, which produced a dull sound.

“Ack! What was that? I didn’t notice it!”

Unlike Mira’s usual thin defenses, Meilin’s body was tough and resistant from all her training, coupled with various Sage Art defenses, so the shield bash barely hurt her.

(I wasn’t even trying to go easy on her… but she didn’t even flinch and even counterattacked. What a fearsome fighting girl.)

Mira knew that Meilin was easily as tough as any warrior class, so she did not hold back when striking her, only to see it had even less effect than she expected.

It had taken blinding and tricking Meilin’s ears to land an attack, only for the Holy Lord that accomplished it to be shattered to pieces by a violent hit a moment later.

The timing and reaction speed of her attacks had improved since the last time Mira had seen her, likely a result of her continued training travels.

Once again, that reminded Mira of how uncommon it was to actually beat Meilin, but it did not discourage her, as she thought up the next thing to try.

“This is getting annoying.”

Meilin continued attempting to attack in Mira’s general direction, while she moved her Holy Lords to never give a direct opening, spreading the attack amongst multiple of them.

The attacks were also gradually growing stronger as Meilin reassessed how much force to use. If she simply went all out, she would easily destroy the Holy Lords, but she was avoiding doing that because she was still a guest in Henry’s home.

Her attacks were powerful enough to destroy a single Holy Lord, but Mira was using multiple of them at once, and the collateral damage from destroying so many of them at once would blow off at least half of the mansion.

Even Meilin was aware of how improper that would be, so instead she tried out a more precise approach with various other attacks, to little avail as the training area was gradually breaking apart as the fight went on.

But it was only a matter of time before Meilin would break free.

“Let’s try this formation next!”

As Mira attempted to experiment with a different lineup of glowing Holy Lords, Meilin had finally found the right amount of strength necessary and created an opening.

Before, her attacks were powerful enough to send a Holy Lord flying back, except that they would be caught and kept in place by the Holy Lords behind it.

But this time she had aimed for the large window on one of the sides of the training area, knocking the Holy Lord out through it.

“How…!”

Meilin had been careful about her movements, ensuring that there was only one row of Holy Knights there, and when she was certain that defenses were thin, she created the perfect opening. She had realized she was at a disadvantage inside there, and found a way to deal with it, and while Mira was in shock by it, Meilin escaped.

“I can finally see again.”

After dealing a finishing blow to the Holy Lord she had knocked out, she stood up and looked at the bright training area, holding her hand out and inviting Mira to come out as well.

“So you got away. Oh well, I’ll play along.”

The battlefield had shifted to the garden outside, and Mira decided that would be the perfect chance to try outdoor tactics and rushed out after Meilin.

+++

# **324: Mira vs. Meilin, cont’d**

The garden of Henry’s mansion was largely a vast lawn, which was also used for training given the wooden dummies spread around.

Most of the plants were kept around the borders, carefully tended to. So while it was an extension of the training area, it also served as a garden to gaze at no matter the season.

But the two opponents hardly saw any of that. Instead, they were in even higher spirits now that they could fight outside.

“I hope you’re ready!”

After a short pause, Meilin gleefully charged ahead.

Mira quickly readied herself for an incoming combo started with Ground Shrink. Meilin’s options were limited now that there were no walls or ceiling, but she could not lower her guard around Meilin, as she knew very well how relentless Meilin was from watching her fight thousands and tens of thousands of times.

But since Mira was so focused on being ready for any possible complex combo, she did not consider that Meilin could do something else coupled with her Ground Shrink advance.

For a moment she realized something was off, and only noticed what it was when it appeared below her.

“What…?!”

She let out a confused voice before a loud crash, after which she was sent flying high into the air. That was an ability Meilin had recently developed, which would start from her feet and creep along the ground before bursting below Mira.

Since it was so new, Mira had not even thought of preparing herself for it.

(So she’s come up with ways to use it as a feint too…!)

Ground Shrink allowed one to rush right next to an opponent, but activating it required a specific foot movement, and with mastery one could mask it amongst other movements, or detect when someone else was trying to use it secretly.

Meilin was one of the best users of it, and now she had found a way to act like she was going to use Ground Shrink, when in reality she was using a different ability, making it much harder to fight her.

After being flung a good ten meters into the air, Mira managed to stabilize herself with Sky Stride, but she was not out of the woods yet.

She felt a sudden burst of mana and almost instinctively used her Summoner Art Evacuation Guidance, bringing all of the Holy Lords she had summoned earlier to her side.

A moment later, a far louder crash than before echoed into the distance.

It was Meilin’s Refined Impact, which she had tried to use on Mira in mid-air, and ended up colliding with the many Holy Lords. It had been so powerful that in the end, only two of the Holy Lords were still in good shape.

“She’s terrifying…”

Mira felt a cold chill as she saw the destruction. But then felt another burst of mana, telling her that Meilin’s combo was not over yet, and Mira desperately kicked around to move away.

The Holy Lords, or what remained of them, did not have that kind of mobility, so gravity took over and pulled them down, but they would not reach the ground.

**Secret Sage Art – Earth: Hazy Azure Moon**

Barely a moment later, an even more powerful blast came from the ground, going in a straight line up.

A powerful gust of wind spread out, the ground below cracked, all the windows rattled, and even the clouds above dispersed in a circular pattern. Meilin’s attack had pierced through the sky, and all the Holy Lords in its path were turned to dust and vanished into the clouds.

(She’s still ridiculously powerful…)

Mira shuddered after experiencing Meilin’s chain of secret abilities as she descended and landed on the mansion’s rooftop, carefully looking at Meilin in case she would continue attacking.

But Meilin showed no signs of moving. Instead, she was looking at Mira completely still, her eyes filled with expectation.

Mira recognized that look. Meilin was essentially saying it was Mira’s turn now. After showing such a powerful attack, she wanted her opponent to also show something impressive.

(And that’s still the same as usual.)

Meilin would no longer attack, and instead was waiting for something exciting to come. Mira smiled seeing that, deciding that was her perfect chance. She had already begun preparations while she was spinning in mid-air, and now she just needed to activate her summons.

“It’s my turn now!”

Mira announced that, and Meilin’s face lit up even more, replying, “Bring it on!”

“As you wish!”

Mira activated her summons, ready to put her experiment into practice, after which countless magic circles appeared in mid-air, covering the sky and being stacked on two layers.

Each of them produced a Dark Knight arm holding weapons, and a moment later they threw those weapons at the ground.

It was similar to what Mira had used against the Skull Dragon in the Ancient Underground City. Except that she had refined and improved it since then.

Now they staggered their timing slightly when throwing their weapons, instead of being all at once, while constantly tracking their target. On top of that, the variety of weapons had increased, including swords, spears, axes, and bows for those who attacked later.

“That’s too much!”

The sky darkened from all the summons, and weapons rained down. That was too much even for Meilin, as her excitement and anticipation quickly turned to panic as she began running around the garden, dodging the incessant stream of weapons following her.

“But I won’t lose!”

Realizing she could not keep running for much longer, she stopped and faced the weapons head on, crossing her arms in front of her face.

“Oh…is she going to do that?”

Seeing that, Mira decided to just throw the remaining weapons all at once, including those from magic circles she had not activated yet. All of that had more than enough power to easily slaughter rank A monsters.

Meanwhile, Meilin stood her ground, staring intently at the weapons going after her. A moment later, all the swords, axes, spears, and arrows fell mercilessly on Meilin. Even the constant dull noise of their collision showed how powerful they were.

“So what do you think? That’s my most recent addition.”

A few seconds later the weapons vanished, revealing Meilin still standing in place, a satisfied smile on her lips.

“That one hit pretty hard! It took me by surprise.”

There was not even a scratch on Meilin as she lowered her arms. She had only been able to survive that onslaught because of the powers of Sages. She had used Sage Fortitude Art: Mountain.

That ability momentarily made it impossible to use Ground Shrink, Sky Stride, and any ranged Heaven Sage Arts, in exchange of an ironclad defense. It also empowered defensive Earth Sage Arts.

She had also used **Sage Art – Earth: Shell** to increase her defenses to the point that the weapons did no damage to her. Having survived all of that, she happily said, “Can you show me anything else you have?”

“Hmm, sure thing. I have just the right thing for you then!”

Meilin wanted to see something even more powerful, something a step above what most knew.

As everything had been done through partial summoning, it did not cost too much mana to use that large attack. A hundred partially summoned weapons cost the same as ten Dark Knights, which was roughly 3% of Mira’s mana pool. Being able to impress Meilin with such a small cost told Mira her experiment had been a big success.

That put her in a good mood, and she happily jumped off the roof to stand in front of Meilin again.

“Are you sure you want to be down here? I’m really tough at close range right now.”

Meilin warned her, or rather made sure she wanted to do that. She was hinting at the fact that **Sage Fortitude Art: Mountain** was still active, making her a much harder foe to fight from close range.

Meanwhile, her ability to deal with ranged opponents was weaker, as she no longer could rely on Ground Shrink or use shockwaves from Heaven Sage Arts.

But Mira ditched her advantage by moving closer, saying, “That’s exactly why I’m coming here.”

That was the perfect chance for Mira to test something of her own. If she could handle Meilin in this state, then she would have no trouble fighting high level magic beasts too. So she really wanted to try out her new abilities.

“Let’s see how you like this one next!”

Mira’s body was enveloped in light as she activated the spell, while Meilin watched attentively with much curiosity.

The swirling mana began to change shape, clinging onto Mira’s body as they revealed the new power brought forth from summoning.

By combining the Holy and Dark Knight Frames, they evolved into the Ashen Knight Frame. And Mira had pushed things even further from that.

Through her research, she had found that the Ashen Knight Frame in theory reacted the same way as any Armor Spirit, and she used that knowledge to evolve her personal abilities even further.

By imbuing the Ashen Knight Frame with the Holy Sword Sanctia, she gained a power no other summoner could use.

**Armor Summoning – Equipment: Sacred Frame**

The light subsided to show Mira clad in a set of armor that gave off a divine shine. The lower half flared out like a skirt, her helmet was shaped like a tiara, and the chest plate was rather small, allowing for better agility.

At first glance, she was reminiscent of the Valkyries, but the shine of her armor was even more dazzling. If anything, that dress-shaped armor was befitting of the queen of Valhalla.

To top it all off, there were two glowing swords floating behind her.

They were both Sanctia, a special holy sword that usually could only be wielded by proficient swordsmen, but that Mira had made accessible to herself through her special summoning.

“I see, that’s what you meant! I feel a lot of power!”

Currently, Mira had become stronger than all the Armor Spirits she had summoned thus far, and Meilin understood why Mira had decided to jump off the roof. Even she believed Mira had evened the playing field, surpassing her expectations.

“Then I also won’t hold back!”

Shouting that, Meilin held her right hand back, gathering mana on it until it began glowing white.

(I’ve never seen her do that before…)

Mira watched warily, as she had never seen that pose or ability before, and all she could do was assume it was a close range attack considering Meilin’s current state.

(Well, I’ll just try hitting back and see what happens.)

At this point, the only way to know what it did was to experience it herself, despite it being a new special ability Meilin had come up with, meaning it was extremely powerful.

Mira adjusted her Frame’s balance to focus on defense and melded a sword of light in her right hand, a stance that would allow her to resist enemy attacks while unleashing a powerful counterattack.

“Come!”

“Let’s do it!”

The two grinned at each other before dashing forward, both of them leaving a bright white trail before they collided in the middle of the garden.

Their special attacks were unleashed at the same time, letting out a blinding flash followed by a deafening explosion. A gale of wind spread out, followed by a shockwave that made everything shake.

In the center of it all were Mira and Meilin, their arms locked in as they glared at each other.

“That’s an interesting ability, but I couldn’t help but notice that streak of light. What was that for?”

Mira had noticed a strange streak of light trailing into the air from Meilin’s fist, and asked about it with a curious voice as she pushed harder against her.

“That’s a secret. But I’m also curious, you’re only holding one sword. What would happen if you used both?”

Meilin refused to answer, and instead glanced briefly at the second sword floating behind Mira, also pushing back with more force.

If one sword had been enough to put them into an even deadlock, then what would happen if Mira used two? Just thinking of that possibility made Meilin shudder with excitement, but her expectations would be shot down.

“Using both? If I could do that, then I would’ve won. But sadly that’s still a work in progress.”

For now, that was only a possibility Mira had not unlocked yet. Mira had given it the temporary name of Light Sword Punch, the special ability of Sacred Frame, but it was still unfinished, and the most she could do was use one of her two swords for it.

“So in short you’re training too?”

“Well, basically yes.”

Research and training were not too different, so Mira nodded in agreement, something that pleased Meilin and filled her with a sense of kinship, as she happily began saying things like, “Yes, there’s nothing better than constant improvement!”

“Mhm… But moving on, shall we go for another bout? I’d love to test out the limits of wielding only one sword.”

Mira eased her arm and took a few steps back, equipping her unspent sword and switching her Frame balance to higher attack output, wanting to see how far she could take things.

“That sounds fun! Let’s do it!”

Meilin replied with a bright smile, jumping back and then taking a few more steps back, creating even more running distance than their previous clash, and then began charging her right hand with mana again.

Since Mira said she wanted to push things further, Meilin was also going to use more strength. But Mira could not sense any change in the amount of mana used, the only difference was the distance between the two.

(Hmm…does she get stronger the more she runs then?)

After evaluating Meilin’s actions, Mira also adjusted her next ability to match that, proportionally to the increase in running distance. Meilin’s ability seemed rather straightforward, but also made it more versatile.

“Ready then?”

“Yes!”

Their eyes locked, they lowered their stance, about to charge at each other again.

“Miraaa, Meimeiii!! Stopppp! That’s enough, please stooooop!!”

But they were stopped by a loud shout, and then they saw Henry running out of the training building from earlier, his arms raised as he desperately put an end to the fight. “If you keep going you’ll really make her cry, so please stop,” he said, quickly glancing in another direction.

Mira and Meilin also looked there and saw her, a maid standing there.

They had been so engrossed in their fight that they had not seen her there, despite her presence the whole time. She was also wearing thick gloves and carried a shovel and a bucket, which likely meant she had been tending to the garden.

Without warning, the garden had suddenly become the main stage for a frightening fight, not even giving her a chance to escape.

And that was not even the worst part. When they got closer to her, they heard her stammering, “The garden…the garden…it’s…it’s…”

That prompted them to look at the state the garden was in. Which had gone from a tidy and pleasant place into a wartorn wilderness.

+++

# **325: Garden Cleanup**

A maid of the Adams Residence stood there, frozen in horror at the sight of the garden ruined by Mira and Meilin’s fight. Her attire also made it clear that she was the maid in charge of the garden, and it did not take long for Mira and Meilin to realize what they had done.

“I’m…uh…sorry about that.”

“Ah…I’m really sorry.”

As their combat high receded, they ran up to the maid and lowered their heads while apologizing profusely.

After that, they volunteered to clean up the garden themselves, starting by flattening out the ravaged ground, gathering the plants and dirt that had gotten blown away, and repairing the fence that had fallen apart, all according to the directions the maid gave them.

While working on that, Martel decided she could not let the opportunity pass up, or maybe she was simply driven by kindness, but whichever the case, she decided to offer her help as well.

By now, Mira had also gotten more used to the power of the Spirit King, so Martel could channel some of her power through it and let Mira use it. That was something Mira happily accepted, and put to use in amending the garden.

“You won’t find anyone better than me when it comes to plants!”

Mira announced that confidently as she began using Martel’s power to reinvigorate the destroyed garden, and to great effect.

Meilin also worked like a mule, quickly amending the pits and hollows of the ground to get it level. Then Mira passed over it with Martel’s power, spreading a vibrant coat of grass over it, which looked even more alive than before their fight.

“It looks so pretty… That’s incredible!”

“I know, I know!”

Vanessa, the maid, was really impressed by the result, which put Mira in a really good mood, after which she went to the outer border past the fence to amend those plants too.

In the end, they also were covered in verdant green leaves, their flowers blooming majestically, and four trees stood tall and firm in each corner of the garden. They were Soul Nuclide trees[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-112123) called Mist Quill, which were known for having flowers that looked like falling feathers. The patriarch of the Adams family, Henry’s father, had brought the seeds from one of his travels to grow them in the garden.

They were known for being tricky to raise, and Vanessa had gone through many troubles just to get them to that size.

So Mira had some advice for her, saying, “If you pour a mana potion on them once a month, their leaves will start to glow faintly making them look even more impressive. You should try that sometime.”

That was a little known reaction produced by the special properties of Mist Quill trees. But all of Martel’s knowledge was freely offered by her.

By that point, Vanessa went from seeing Mira as a rowdy summoner that ruined her garden into thinking of her as a plant specialist. “I’ll try it out tonight!” she said with excitement, before letting out a short, “Ah,” and running off somewhere. Moments later, she came back holding three black seeds.

“So I have these, but…”

Those seeds had also been brought there by Henry’s father, but all he knew was that they came from some fruit he ate at a party, and very little else.

He had simply fallen in love with those fruits when he ate them, so he brought back the seeds. The fruit had been served cut into small pieces, so he did not even know what the full fruit looked like, or what color it was, all he knew was that it tasted good.

At least he had tried to get some information from the party’s host, who did not want to give out much information as it was something really rare, and just boasted about it.

“I tried planting them at different times and in different soil a lot of times, and I managed to get them to sprout five times, but without fail they always dried off shortly after… I really don’t know what I’m doing wrong.”

The seeds also looked really plain, so it was impossible to gain much knowledge from looking at them either.

After her many attempts, she was left with only three of them, at which point she stopped trying to grow them until she knew more about them. But Henry’s father was still looking forward to trying that fruit again, so Vanessa felt constant pressure to grow them somehow, and finally saw some hope now that Mira was there.

“Hmm… I guess servants have their own sorts of trouble then…”

Mira thought back to Lily and the other maids she knew, who fulfilled a similar role but seemed to have way too much free time in their hands. But Vanessa here was in a more difficult position.

“Let me take a look at them.”

As a sense of impending dread gradually grew stronger in Mira’s mind, she took one of the seeds and examined it closely.

It was an oval shaped seed, roughly the size of a thumb, and that was about it. Nothing uncommon about it, and it would not look out of place just sitting around in the wilderness.

‘That’s the seed of a King Tree Apple. I’m sure of it!’

As expected, the mother of all nature, Martel, knew instantly what it was, and also could pinpoint right away why all of Vanessa’s attempts had failed.

“I see, these seeds are…”

Mira began relaying everything Martel had told her, acting like she had always been really knowledgeable about it.

That seed had come from a special fruit called the King Tree Apple. And while it was called an apple, its texture was closer to that of a melon, while its outer hide was thin like an apple’s, making it really delicate, and difficult to grow while ensuring the fruits could ripen enough.

“But there’s something really important you should know if you still want to grow them.”

It would still take a long time of hardships before new fruits could be obtained.

Mira carefully explained all of that, but Vanessa did not seem distraught by it, and instead was filled with motivation to try again. So Mira told her the most important detail when growing them, “After they sprout, they can’t receive any light at all until they grow up to three meters tall.”

“No…light at all?”

Vanessa was really shocked to hear that, which was understandable. It was common knowledge that plants and fruits needed plenty of sunlight to grow strong and tasty. But Mira, or rather Martel, said this was an exception.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. TLN: Soul Nuclide is apparently the name for plants with mana regeneration properties

Those trees were native to a remote forest in the shade of a God Tree, a place with many tall trees obscuring most of the light, so the young saplings adapted to growing under such conditions, in turn becoming weak to light. That was the main reason why Vanessa kept failing to grow them.

“I had no idea plants like that existed…”

Vanessa stared at the seeds in shock, and Mira tried to comfort her saying, “They’re extremely rare seeds, so they require special treatment.”

Martel was also a bit taken aback that one of her plants had become so weak to light.

At first, she had created those trees with the intention to feed animals in a place where the only things in reach were dead and rotten leaves.

The forest around the God Tree was thick and dark, protected by a divine power that made it a paradise for animals. But as one got closer to the God Tree, the darker it got, and the harder it was for trees to bear fruit. The stronger animals would usually stay in the outer parts, but the weaker ones had no choice but to venture deeper to stay safe.

So Martel created a fruit so the weakest animals could eat properly as well, one that did not require light to ripen properly. As time passed and the trees became accustomed to that environment, they began to lose their strength against light while young.

Martel had been in a rather good mood as she told that story, as she also enjoyed seeing how her creations changed and evolved over time in different environments. She was also rather proud that the fruits had a much stronger scent now, making them easier to find by animals.

“By the way, how long does it take until they grow to three meters tall?”

Earlier, Mira had mentioned that the trees had to be kept away from light until they were three meters tall, which meant that they could be exposed to light after that. That was also something Martel had shared with Mira, as by that point the bark on the tree would be thick enough to offer protection from light.

“Around two years. But it’ll take three to six years more before it starts to produce fruits.”

It would take at least five years, during two of which the tree could not be exposed to light. It really was a tree not meant to grow in the same environment as people.

“So at least five years…and the first two are the most important…”

Despite the difficulty, Vanessa showed no signs of giving up. Rather, she was already thinking about building a pitch black room to keep the saplings in for two years, and the best way to care for them in the darkness.

“Oh, you won’t have to worry about that too much.”

Saying that, Mira held her hand over the three seeds, letting out a faint glow that was absorbed into them.

“What was that?”

Vanessa looked anxious at the seeds, and Mira explained, “I’ve invigorated the seeds, so they should grow to three meters tall in just a week.”

That was the result of Martel’s kindness, and her severity. She had seen how much Vanessa wanted to grow those trees, and she did not want to allow any more saplings to dry out.

“Think of this as a gift from a plant spirit I’ve formed a Contract with. Take good care of them.”

Mira did not specify that she was talking about an Originator Spirit. It was already a known fact that she had contracts with plenty of spirits, and she was not lying either, so it was a safe way of talking about it without risking revealing too much.

“Thank you, thank you so much! I promise I’ll grow them into tall and strong trees!

After passing on Martel’s thoughts in a roundabout way, Vanessa thanked her and then added, “Also say thank you to that spirit for me,” while repeatedly bowing to Mira.

‘Oh, you’re very welcome.’

Martel sounded almost embarrassed, but still happy as her response echoed in Mira’s head.

After nearly destroying the garden of the Adams Residence, it was rebuilt to look even better than it did before, while fitting even closer to Vanessa’s ideal vision.

On top of that, the Mist Quill trees that Vanessa had been struggling with had grown into large magnificent trees, and then she even learned how to take care of the mystery seeds that had put her in such a conundrum before.

By the end of that, Mira had gained the respect and trust of Vanessa, who happened to be a maid in a high position, so in the end, her opinion of Mira was shared and spread amongst the other maids as well.

(Alright, I think I managed to gloss things over!)

Thanks to their work, there were no signs of their fight left in the garden, and they would not be questioned about it anymore. Or at least, Mira hoped so as she let out a sigh of relief. She could only imagine the scolding she would get if word spread and Solomon caught wind of it.

Her fight with Meilin did have a strong effect on the people of the mansion though.

Meilin had been staying there for a while, training the children of the mansion in exchange for housing, so they had taken notice of Meilin’s incredible strength. Now they had seen Mira fight Meilin on equal footing, which left a strong impression on them.

Now that she had gained the respect of so many of them, the Adams Residence would always welcome her.

There were no objections to letting her come in too, and now she was in Meilin’s room, alone with her.

“By the way, why did you come here, _Grandfather_? Are you also going to take part in the tournament?”

All that fighting and gardening had taken a toll, so they sat exhausted on a couch, and those were Meilin’s first words. Grandfather…that was not really the way one would address a girl like Mira. But Meilin had not stuttered, so Mira dejectedly replied, “So you could tell it was me.”

“Of course. The way you shift your weight when stepping forward, the way you run, and the way you’re constantly looking around, it’s all exactly the same as before. You can change how you look, but you can’t deceive me.”

Meilin explained how she had seen through Mira, while also emphasizing that those were just a few examples of the tells she noticed.

And she had not even needed to see any of the summons to know that much, which usually were the easiest way to tell Mira was Danbulf. Mira’s demeanor alone was enough.

“So you could tell from just that… You never cease to amaze me.”

Meilin had not lost any of her keen perception, so Mira commended her on that before standing up straight and saying, “So about the reason why I’m here…”

+++

# **326: Transformation**

“And that’s why I was searching for you, to bring you back to our country. It took so much effort since there’s no way of contacting you…”

Mira gave a brief explanation about the current state of their country and the Nine Wisemen. In response, Meilin looked rather sullen, as she really wanted to keep traveling.

(That side of her hasn’t changed at all either…)

Meilin’s emotions were always obvious on her face, just like they were way back when.

She had never been able to stay in their country even during the game days. If there was any type of battle, they would let her know and she would come back immediately, but they pretty much had to find her and drag her along for any other type of event. Other than that, she was always absent from Arkite.

“Ah, if everyone else is there then I’m sure you’ll be fine. You can just cover for me!”

After a long time thinking, she said that like she had just come up with a really bright idea.

That was pretty much the reaction Mira had expected. They were only gathering to avoid a potential invasion, standing proudly as a symbol of peace for their country. So Meilin did not feel like it was worth her time to be there.

But she could not forget that she was still part of the Nine Wisemen, and more importantly, this world was real now.

Mira was fully aware of that, so much to her chagrin, she could not afford to be lenient with Meilin.

“If you really don’t want to come back, then I understand. But there’s still another issue…”

She began by showing a bit of kindness, saying it was not fully necessary for Meilin to be back, before cornering her right away.
