“I would’ve never expected that you were looking into them as well, Alma. I had heard that things were getting unstable for them lately, and now I understand why.”

The Fifty Bells were also spread across the continent with a strong information network, so Kagura not only knew about Ira Muerte, but had a grasp on their internal affairs. She knew they had been suffering various losses recently, creating the perfect opening to attack.

“Yes, I’ll happily help out with anything that you need. We’ve also gathered some information that might be of use, so I’ll bring that over when I can.”

Kagura was more than willing to help them, and not just with the interrogation, but with anything else that could be needed. Partly because of her sense of justice, and mostly because Ira Muerte was a known collaborator of Chimera Clauzen.

The Fifty Bells had continued chasing after the remnants of Chimera Clauzen, while investigating all the organizations that had ties to them. Ira Muerte came up time and time again, but they were quite resilient, making it difficult to investigate them.

Almost by a stroke of luck, Alma’s request turned out to be exactly what Kagura needed all that time.

“Thank you, Kagura!”

Regardless of the reasons why, Alma was delighted to hear Kagura’s response and once again tackled her with a hug. Mira once again watched them with a smile.

(And that’s another accomplishment in my name.)

The capture of Jorg and Kagura’s arrival only happened because of Mira, and that had resulted in Nirvana and the Fifty Bells forming an alliance.

Mira realized that Alma owed her a lot now, so she began to think of ways to use that to her advantage, like arranging an intermission during the most exciting moment of the tournament, to perform a demonstration of summoning.

With Kagura there, only one step remained between them and Jorg’s interrogation, for which the three of them visited the palace’s tearoom.

“It’s finally time, Noin.”

They were there to find Noin, who sat with some tea and snacks on a table, reading a comic book. He had been taking it quite easy while he waited for his next mission, after being discharged from being the oracle’s bodyguard.

“Ah, Alma, good job as usual.”

He turned around as he replied, his face contorting quizzically as soon as he noticed Mira was also there, only to be overtaken by surprise when he also saw Kagura there, jumping on his feet as he exclaimed, “Woah! Is that you Kagura?!”

“It’s been a while, Noin.”

Hearing her voice, Noin looked rather reassured as he smiled at her.

“Yes, it has been. I’m glad we could meet again.”

Thirty years had passed since the last time they had seen each other, but seeing that Kagura had not changed in that time filled him with delight and old memories, even as he constantly fought his instincts that drew him to look at Mira.

With Noin joining them, the four of them finally headed to their main destination.

It had been no coincidence that they had run into Noin there.

They were headed to a special high security jail, so it did not matter if Alma was the empress, she had to enter with someone authorized, or if anything, being the empress was the reason why she needed to be guarded.

As a result, Noin, who also held the key to the jail, had to accompany her.

“It’s not like I’ll even see any action with this lineup…”

He briefly looked at Mira and Kagura behind Alma, two of the Nine Wisemen who could keep Alma just as safe as him. Then again, that was only evident to Noin who knew them. Anyone else only saw three defenseless ladies attempting to visit the jail. They would only be let in if they were accompanied by one of the Twelve Apostles like Noin.

The special jail was situated slightly to the north of the first floor’s center, inside of the guards’ barracks. Getting there meant passing through a security check by the barrack’s captain, who at first seemed hesitant to let Alma, Mira, and Kagura enter the jail, but let them in when he saw Noin.

Soon the three arrived at the entrance of the jail.

“Your turn to shine, Noin.”

“Alright, I’m on it.”

A robust metallic door blocked their way, and only a handful of people had the keys to open it.

Noin unlocked it, revealing a long descending staircase behind it. The special jail was situated deep below Nirvana’s imperial palace. That place was used to contain criminals with noble blood, or prisoners considered politically or militarily important.

The black tiles set onto the floor were not just for looks either, a spell that reported the position of those walking around back to the guards’ barracks was imbued into them for added security.

The walls and ceiling were white, and the cells were made entirely of iron bars with no walls, providing next to no privacy. Everything was well lit as well, giving ample visibility, making one forget this was a prison if not for the cells.

“This is far more lively than I was expecting.”

While not exactly noisy, the voices of prisoners talking could be heard constantly. Mira had expected a more desolate place for the jail, considering how rarely such a secure place would be used. But a decent number of cells were occupied.

“We’ve gotten a pretty big haul recently, thanks to you both.”

A mix of taunts and pleas for mercy came from the cells as they passed by as well, while Alma threw a playful look to Mira and Kagura.

As she explained, half of the prisoners were highly influential people whose ties to Chimera Clauzen had been exposed, kept there to allow for proper and careful investigations.

The other half were the assassins Mira captured before. There were so many of them who all came at the same time, that most of them had not been identified yet, so they were kept there for the time being.

“So they had spread this much here as well.”

Kagura’s scornful eyes surveyed the Chimera Clauzen members there. Even after some time, her feelings towards them remained the same.

“Seeing so many cells occupied feels a bit…”

Mira was rather bemused by the state of the prison, unsure of whether that was proof of how proactive the guards were, or just how far crime had spread.

They continued discussing things like that as they reached further into the prison, reaching yet another special area. It was an empty room, around six tatami mats in size. There were only the lights inlaid into the ceiling, and five steel doors along the solid stone walls.

One of those doors led to the cell where Jorg was held, as Alma explained while walking up to it.

“Let me open it.”

Noin followed right after, unlocking the door and opening it to reveal just how unique those cells were.

“Now this is really secure too.”

It was a long narrow room, more like a corridor, barely wide enough for two people to stand next to each other, going around ten meters deep. Three iron bar doors stood in the way of the other end of the room as well.

“But it’s still nothing compared to her room.”

Alma joked in return, while still being fully confident that no prisoner would ever manage to escape from there.

The walls were reinforced with a special metal alloy, making it impossible to dig out and escape. The iron bars were the same, resistant even to a raid boss, according to Alma. All of the locks required a different key as well, as Noin had to unlock each other to let the girls pass.

Only when they got to the last set of iron bars were they able to see Jorg.

He was in a straitjacket, completely restrained to a platform, his mouth gagged, a blindfold covering his eyes, and thick earmuffs shutting away all sound from reaching his ears.

And that was not all. The walls, floor, and ceiling of the deepest area were all covered in familiar symbols.

“Those symbols everywhere…aren’t they the same as those on Arresting Cloth?”

Mira had seen those symbols on the pieces of cloth she used to stop captives from using magic. They were providing a similar effect in this cell, though a bit more sophisticated.

“Yup, they are.”

Alma nodded, explaining how she had tested various methods before settling on that one.

Stepping past the last set of iron bars was enough for their effect to activate, acting the same as if one was wrapped in Arresting Cloth. Only the person holding the key remained unaffected.

So Noin alone passed through, picking up Jorg to bring him closer to the iron bars, within range of Kagura’s spell.

Jorg quickly caught onto what was happening, as he began jostling around and trying to resist, creating a mix of creaks and bumps as he hit the platform. Mira and Alma stepped back, startled by the sudden movements, but Kagura remained composed.

As the founder of the Fifty Bells, and the sole spellcaster able to use that interrogation spell, she had seen similar sights countless times, as she coldly stared at Jorg through the iron bars.

Regaining her composure, Alma nodded at Kagura, who replied in kind and held up a paper charm, activating her interrogation spell.

+++

# **345: Unveiling Truth**

Jorg had been trained to resist interrogation, no matter what torture he endured. And despite that, he was entirely at the mercy of Kagura’s spell. His groans and efforts to wrest himself free also stopped once the spell activated, calmly answering anything Alma asked.

Kagura focused only on keeping the spell active, while Alma did the rest.

The first questions were simple and direct, only to verify that Jorg was truly under the spell, after which Kagura moved onto more important ones. And surely enough, Jorg quickly spat out a lot of vital information.

“This is incredible…”

“I know, I know!”

Noin had seen how much Jorg resisted during previous interrogations, never speaking a single word, so seeing him spilling the beans so quickly almost made him shudder. Meanwhile Mira puffed her chest, proud that it was a fellow Wiseman that had accomplished this.

Alma also scribbled down all of the important information that came out. The more she heard, the more she could feel the shroud of mystery pulling back, revealing what had puzzled her in the past.

“Tell me the name, occupation, and nationality of every person you’ve met in Ira Muerte.”

“The ones…I know…in Ira Muerte…”

Jorg’s response was immediate.

He began listing the names of people tied to the organization, who came from all walks of life. Some of those names produced shocked reactions from Alma and Noin too.

Nobles, adventurers and mercenaries were evident enough, followed by blacksmiths, arms dealers, pharmacists and Magic Wares dealers, even the owners of rather boutique shops were mentioned, followed by a long stream of merchant names.

Alma and Noin personally knew many of those merchants as well, who looked betrayed to hear that someone they believed was trustworthy had been involved. And that was only the beginning of the information Kagura’s spell provided.

“Tell me all of the jobs you did for the organization.”

“My jobs…I killed…lots…”

Jorg had made a name for himself as an assassin in the underside of society, so his jobs were to kill anyone who tried to get in the way of the organization. And he confessed to all of it.

One after another, he listed the names of his victims, as well as how he killed them.

His methods were those of a professional. He hardly ever used blades, or even directly touched his victims. Everything was staged to look like an accident or sudden illness, disguising the fact that it was a targeted assassination.

That made him priceless to the organization, as they deployed him everywhere they could, and the list of victims continued to grow past twenty names. It did not take long to reach thirty either.

“I knew she didn’t just get sick randomly.”

“You did it… so it was all you…!”

Sophia Tinfield. The moment that name escaped Jorg’s lips, Alma and Noin became irate, full of resentment.

“Now you’ll know what it feels to—”

“Noin!”

That was too much. Noin lunged forward like a vengeful spirit, and Alma had to stop him before he reached Jorg’s throat. Even then, Alma was also gritting her teeth, her clenched fists trembling with rage.

Clearly Sophia Tinfield was someone dear to both of them, who had been killed under the guise of a sudden illness.

Mira could not even begin to imagine what they felt, as this was the first time she had seen either of them this upset. All she could do was to stay calm and be ready to intervene if their emotions became too strong to control.

Once Noin calmed down a bit, Alma resumed asking questions.

In the end, the tally of people killed under Ira Muerte’s orders totaled fifty three. It was a painful number to process, but looking into the reasons why they had been killed could provide insight into Ira Muerte’s plans, so it was valuable information.

He also revealed the communication methods of Ira Muerte.

They had members called Linkers, who specialized in relaying messages and orders from their headquarters to the field. They were also responsible for returning with updates and reports.

That meant that by capturing a Linker, they would secure a wealth of information, spanning deep into the organization as a whole.

---

“Alright, let’s start by condensing the information we got.”

Two hours and some minutes after Jorg’s interrogation began, they had heard everything they needed to know, and went to Alma’s room to review everything.

Esmeralda also joined them on the way back, who also rejoiced at seeing Kagura again, showering her with affection, and Kagura did not really seem to mind it, likely thanks to Esmeralda’s maternal nature.

Then came their analysis and planning meeting. The notepad with everything Alma jotted down was on the table, and they went in order from the first page. There was a goldmine of information there, and if utilized properly it would guide them all the way to the core of the organization.

For now, their biggest hurdle was the source of their information, an induced confession from one person. They still needed to find ways of proving all of that.

“I guess having such a large country also comes with its share of issues.”

Considering Nirvana’s size, it was no surprise that various of the adventurers stationed there were also connected to Ira Muerte. The empire covered a vast area, including those adventurers who preferred to hunt and explore. And with increased numbers, it was unavoidable that some would be rotten.

“Maybe it would be best to consult with the Union leader about this.”

“That’s true, let’s proceed like that then.”

Tracking down adventurers was difficult, as they tended to travel constantly. So Esmeralda suggested getting help from the Union, and Alma agreed.

“Ah, this person. I feel like I’ve seen that name before… Yes, we got them too.”

Kagura was looking through the list of merchants when she suddenly brought forth a list of her own from her Item Box. As it turned out, some of the merchants connected to Ira Muerte had also been dealing with Chimera Clauzen.

“Nice catch, Kagura. Now we can bring them in for their involvement with Chimera, and then ambush them about Ira Muerte.”

Alma was delighted to hear that, so then she checked with Kagura for more matches like that. There were still many efforts underway to capture the remnants of Chimera Clauzen, with new arrests being carried out daily.

Meanwhile, there was little known about Ira Muerte, and Jorg’s testimony was not enough to carry out a proper arrest. So it was better to bring them in due to their connection to Chimera Clauzen first.

That had the added effect of masking their pursuit of Ira Muerte, making it seem they were looking for something else.

“Ah, here! This one could work too!”

It was no surprise that merchants that were involved with one corrupt group joined others, so soon Alma was picking out more and more names that appeared in both lists.

That went on for a while longer.

Then they went on to review the list of assassination victims, thought up plans to capture a Linker, and compiled all of it into more digestible files, which would be provided to the intelligence agencies.

After some time talking like that…

“This could work.”

Alma highlighted one name on the list.

He was another merchant, who appeared like a common and regular merchant. But he had a secret, one revealed by Jorg. He acted like a Linker, and was also involved in selling a variety of highly illegal items in the black market.

“Let’s get him to help us out.”

A grin spread on Alma’s lips as she thought of a plan, a frigid light deep in her eyes as she explained it.

(A lure huh… I can see it working out so that’s good enough.)

Once they wrapped up their discussion, Mira headed back to the oracle’s room. Alma and Esmeralda called an urgent meeting with the government’s higherups, to share the compiled information and their plans.

Kagura’s role was complete too, so she returned to the inn where Tiriel was waiting for her. But she knew that they might need her help again, so she left behind her white tiger shikigami Gautarou, which shrunk to the size of a kitten to stay with Alma.

Whenever they needed Kagura again, Alma could just summon her through Gautarou.

“Uhmm, I think it’s like this…”

Mira stood in front of the large gates leading to the oracle’s room, where she brandished the key Alma gave her, and tried to follow the instructions she wrote down.

Past all the gates and doors, she rushed through the garden, heading to the living room where she left Iris.

“This is bad, meow… I’ve used up everything I had… But it’s meow’s life motto to always find a way out!”

“Wow, that was really good! I really thought I had you there! It’s only a matter of time though!”

Two lively voices could be heard from the living room.

They were the First Lieutenant and Iris, clearly having fun with whatever they were doing.

“I see you’re having fun over here.”

Mira entered the living room, glad that Iris was in a good mood, who quickly replied, “Welcome back!” while beaming a warm smile.

“Yes, I’m back.”

Mira could not stifle a smile seeing Iris like that. She also took note of what Iris was holding, which explained why the two were having so much fun. Both of them were holding cards, with more of them piled up all over the table.

The two were currently duking it out in a match of Legend of Astelia.

Mira had left them watching the final matches of the tournament that morning, which likely influenced them to play. They had been going at it for quite a while, as the First Lieutenant’s sign had a record of their previous matches.

So far Iris remained undefeated. There had been a few close calls, but all of them always ended with the First Lieutenant’s defeat.

“There has been neowthing to report!”

The First Lieutenant jumped on his feet to salute and indicate he had properly protected Iris.

“Good, you did well.”

Mira nodded approvingly, the scene in front of her nothing if not peaceful. She approached the table, taking a closer look at the cards just as the finishing blow was dealt.

“And this is check mate!”

“I’ve lost againnn!!”

The card Iris used sealed the deal. The First Lieutenant spun back in an exaggerated defeat motion, soon after getting back up while mumbling, “This is all just a difference in experience meow,” trying to explain away his loss.

And that was not the end, as he followed it with, “There have to be better cards!” and dove straight into the pile of cards.

Mira took note of a large box placed on a corner of the table, which had not been there that morning. It was surrounded by many cards as well, all owned by Iris. She was lending those to the First Lieutenant, so he could have a deck to play.

Meanwhile she was sticking to a couple of fully built decks, which she kept in cases near her.

In other words, Iris had been using her polished and refined decks, while the First Lieutenant had to quickly improvise his. So it was no surprise that he kept losing. That was how Mira interpreted the situation, until Iris dropped a truth bomb.

“He’s actually doing really well, he’s an amazing player! He’s been putting up a really good fight despite having never played before. I’d say he’s already better than Noin! His main shortcoming is the main card of his deck. For now a summoner deck is a bit tricky to play out, maybe he would do better with the Vice-Wiseman Creos or Ocean King Deepsea Avalanche cards, but those are really rare so I don’t have them.”

Iris had actually played against him, so she had a better grasp of his ability. In her eyes, he was extremely talented to play this well while using an improvised deck and playing for the first time.

But what struck Mira the most were the rest of her words.

“That can’t…be…”

The card game was mirroring reality in a cruel way. Summoners were in a harsh position. After all, Legend of Astelia had been modeled off the real world. So with no summoners standing out, they also had a minimal role in the game.

While Mira stared blankly, horrified by that realization, Iris continued to comment how the First Lieutenant would win in the blink of an eye if he switched to a Magician deck.

The First lieutenant quickly reacted to those words, filled with new motivation.

“That does it then. I’ll come back with a completely new deck neow!”

Saying that, he threw aside his summoner deck and began building a new one.

The discarded cards were carefully picked up by Mira, who looked at them while internally debating on visiting the company producing the game, and terrorizing…or rather educating them on how powerful summoners actually were.

++++

# **Reborn as a Transcendent - Chapter 713 - I’ve Already Seen Through Your Schemes!**

“Sis!”

“Princess!”

At that moment, two pleasant voices shattered the strange silence that had blanketed the scene. Pixie and Mylene hurried over with relieved expressions on their faces. They had thought Yae-hime must have encountered some terrible danger.

But as the two drew close, they realized something was wrong. Yae-hime’s complexion was unusually pale. On closer inspection, they could see her hand trembling slightly, and the aura she released was uneven and disordered. It was clear her condition was far from good.

Just as Mylene and Pixie were about to speak, Yae-hime opened her mouth first. “Mylene, help me keep my phone and the terminal.”

Even before her words had faded, she handed over an object about the size of a power bank. It was none other than the game’s terminal. Anticipating sudden incidents that might occur inside the game, she always carried it with her.

Besides that, she also passed over a Huawhey phone.

“Sis…” Mylene accepted them with visible worry.

Seeing this, Yae-hime slowly shook her head. “Don’t worry, I just need a little rest.” Though she said that, her complexion grew increasingly worse.

“If it really doesn’t work out, I can take your place,” Pixie offered.

“No, I can handle it.” Yae-hime waved her hand lightly, but a faint trickle of crimson suddenly slipped from the corner of her lips. That hardly looked like she was fine at all!

Mylene and Pixie were instantly overwhelmed with worry.

Let’s go back a little in time.

“Ow… that hurts!” Yae-hime had been blasted away by that surge of spatial power, crashing heavily into the water. She nearly blacked out completely. Fortunately, her physique was incredibly resilient, and she managed to endure it.

Her clothes, however, had not been so fortunate. The brand-new sportswear she wore was almost torn to shreds by the impact. And that was even with Yae-hime guarding it with all her strength.

Yet compared to her appearance, the real damage lay within. That single instant when the space collapsed had dealt her grave injuries. Had it been an ordinary grandmaster, they would have died outright.

“Cough!” She spat out a mouthful of blood, her face turning deathly pale. “This situation is bad.” A quick internal examination revealed her body was in complete disarray.

At that moment, the Green Emperor’s Longevity Art had already begun circulating, swiftly repairing her body.

“I should head ashore first.” Remembering that she still had to duel Lucky later, Yae-hime turned her gaze toward Baiding Island. “Thankfully, I brought my bag along, otherwise this would be a real problem.”

Scooping up the Adidas shoulder bag floating nearby, she glanced at her tattered outfit and let out a helpless smile. When the space had collapsed, Yae-hime had borne the brunt of the impact directly, so the bag had come through mostly unscathed. The items inside were likely intact as well.

Enduring the searing pain, she swam ashore and quickly slipped into the forest. After scanning her surroundings and confirming no one was nearby, she opened the bag. And immediately froze.

She clearly remembered packing a spare set of sportswear, so why had it turned into a set of ancient garments?! Not only that, but even shoes and hair ornaments were included!

“Little Blue, I’m going to spank you!” After a brief thought, she immediately knew who the culprit was. Aside from that mischievous little one, no one else would dare meddle with her belongings.

“Oh well, better than having nothing to wear.” Glancing at her shredded clothing, Yae-hime sighed softly.

The outfit was a custom piece prepared by Nangong Lin. She had originally planned to wear it on a formal occasion, yet here she was, forced to put it on now.

“This Little Blue is far too cheeky.” After changing, Yae-hime muttered irritably.

Fortunately, this time it had turned out to be an ancient dress. If it had been a bunny-girl outfit, she would have gone back and spanked that culprit until their backside swelled. In a sense, a bunny-girl costume would have been even more humiliating than the rags she had just been wearing.

Inside the shoulder bag, there was also a phone and the terminal, both sealed tightly inside vacuum bags. Upon opening them, she saw that the phone was fine, able to power on. As for the terminal, there was not a scratch on it. In fact, damaging it would have been a far greater challenge.

She checked the time. Less than eight minutes remained until seven o’clock.

“There’s no time for me to slowly recover.” From here to the plaza, there was still quite a distance. If she wanted to make it on time, she could only push herself and hurry over. “If I show up late for the duel, I’ll definitely be mocked with sarcastic words.”

Although Yae-hime cared little for other people’s opinions, she still found it necessary to arrive on time. After all, she was a punctual person.

In the end, Yae-hime reached the plaza with only seconds left on the countdown. Hesitating for a moment, she chose to seize the initiative by making a grand entrance. That would buy her a little more time to recover.

It also satisfied her urge to show off. If one lived without a little flair, wasn’t that no different from being a salted fish? Thus, the spectacle they had just witnessed was born.

The effect was astonishing, granting her precious recovery time. Had Mylene and Pixie not called out to her earlier, the results would have been even better.

“This is my duel with her. Irrelevant people, stand aside!” Lucky suddenly barked out. Seeing Yae-hime appear in such a flamboyant way left him deeply displeased. He felt his martial heart had been sullied by her petty tricks.

Mylene rolled her eyes at him, while Pixie pretended not to hear.

“You two wait over there for a bit. I’ll be right back,” Yae-hime said softly.

“Princess, take care.”

“Sis, good luck!”

Although both were worried, they respected her wishes.

“Don’t think I don’t know what you’re up to,” Lucky suddenly spoke again. His booming voice spread across the plaza. Everyone present heard it clearly.

“What am I up to?” Since her opponent wanted a war of words, Yae-hime was more than happy to oblige. It would help her gain even more time to recover. If they clashed immediately, her injuries would become impossible to conceal.

“You deliberately waited until the last moment to pull that little stunt, all to shake my martial heart. You wanted me to fight timidly, second-guessing myself. Too bad, your scheme has already been seen through!” Lucky pointed directly at Yae-hime, his face full of self-assured confidence.

She was momentarily dumbfounded. Her flashy entrance had only been to show off a little and, more importantly, to buy time. By walking from midair to the center of the plaza, she had gained a precious dozen seconds. Now, her injuries had recovered by nearly two-fifths.

Not far away, in what could loosely be called the spectator’s area…

“That so-called void walk just now, she must have used some kind of tool,” one grandmaster from Korea remarked uncertainly.

“I once saw a video of the Princess fighting. I was especially impressed when she used her flying sword. I’ve heard Cathay has arts for controlling swords and objects. She most likely used one of those mystical techniques to put on a show.” Grandmaster Ota spoke with a serious expression.

The crowd, upon hearing this, found his words to be quite reasonable.

‘I used to need external tools just to walk in the air. But things are different now.’ Yae-hime’s lips curved slightly as she thought to herself.

Through this accident, her understanding of spatial power had advanced to a higher level. What she displayed as Void Walk was but a surface glimpse of that insight.

“Hmph. No matter how clever your tricks, you will die beneath my hands. Come!” Lucky clenched both fists, one in front and one behind his chest, then stomped his left foot down. The powerful aura of an intermediate grandmaster erupted instantly.

“Then come.” Yae-hime stood ramrod straight like a spear, casually extending her right hand as she replied in an indifferent tone.

A battle between grandmasters officially began!

+++

# **714 – The Might of a Grandmaster, Truly Frightening**

The entire scene fell silent as everyone held their breath. A tense atmosphere spread through the air.

Lucky did not waste words. His expression hardened with focus, and with a forceful step of his left foot, his body shot forward like a launched projectile. It was like a 107mm shell!

Seeing this, Yae-hime dared not be careless. In an instant, she snapped to full alertness.

In the blink of an eye, Lucky charged with lightning speed. His tightly clenched right fist suddenly swung out, aimed directly at Yae-hime’s head. Even before the fist reached her, the violent force of the punch blew her hair and ribbons into the air.

Faced with such a sharp strike, Yae-hime did not retreat but advanced instead. She stepped forward swiftly, her slender hand reaching out to strike against Lucky’s arm with force.

Two mighty forces collided, producing a muffled boom.

To everyone’s surprise, Lucky was driven into disadvantage in this very first exchange. With Yae-hime’s push, his stance was immediately thrown off balance.

Seizing the moment, she clenched her fist and countered with a strike of her own. Her target was also his head!

The audience present and many watching the livestream were struck with disbelief. But the true experts among them remained calm, as though everything was within their expectations.

Just as Yae-hime’s fist shot out, a sly smile appeared on Lucky’s lips. The next instant, his figure blurred and vanished before her eyes.

From the spectators’ perspective, Yae-hime was now completely exposed, her guard wide open. She was in an extremely dangerous predicament!

At that very moment, Lucky reappeared behind her, his body whipping into a lightning-fast roundhouse kick. His target was the same as before, her unguarded head.

‘The match is over!’ someone thought to themselves.

Such speed, such ferocity! There was no way that Princess could react in time. The battle was decided. Many shared that conclusion. Some even shook their heads inwardly. They had expected an exciting duel, yet victory seemed settled in just two moves.

Still, watching a Grandmaster, and such a beautiful Grandmaster at that, be struck down on the spot was thrilling enough. It was worth the ticket.

However, they were clearly deluding themselves. Just as Lucky’s kick was about to land on Yae-hime’s head, a bizarre sight unfolded. The figure of Yae-hime standing there twisted and distorted under the force of the sweeping kick.

And then, though his leg followed through, Lucky felt only empty air beneath his strike!

“Not good!” At almost the same instant, a fierce aura surged from behind him. Without a second thought, Lucky twisted his body with brute force, crossing his arms before his chest in defense.

A dark shadow struck, swooping down like an eagle snatching a chick, and delivered a sharp kick onto Lucky’s forearms. With a resounding crash, Lucky was blasted backward, his face flashing with astonishment.

The shadow—Yae-hime—landed steadily without pressing the attack further. For she knew very well that in the instant her kick had connected, Lucky had already stamped the ground, propelling himself backward to disperse the force of her strike.

In other words, he had taken no real damage at all, and chasing after him would have been pointless. Moreover, she needed time to recover from her injuries. Every second she could stall was precious.

The scene fell silent for a moment, then erupted in gasps of astonishment.

“How did she do that?!”

“Incredible!”

“She was right in front a moment ago, how did she suddenly appear in midair?!”

“So this is a Grandmaster’s battle? I’m hooked!”

Just a few seconds of exchange had already sent the spectators’ adrenaline surging. Though most could not truly follow what was happening, the sheer beauty of a battle transcending human limits stirred their hearts deeply.

This was true combat!

The experts present showed mild surprise, but after thinking it through, they found it perfectly reasonable. This was merely a warm-up.

“I see now. As expected of a young Grandmaster, you do have some skill,” Lucky said calmly, steadying his stance and gazing at Yae-hime.

“You’re not bad either,” she replied casually.

For now, she did not mind indulging in a little mutual flattery if it could buy her more time to restore her strength to its peak. But clearly, Lucky had no intention of playing along.

“Unfortunately, you won’t live past today. No, you absolutely won’t survive three minutes!” As soon as his words fell, the immense aura within Lucky erupted outward, spreading like a violent storm.

The spectators felt a sudden gale sweep over them, many instinctively raising their arms to shield themselves. Only the true experts stood firm, unmoving, their eyes fixed straight ahead.

‘Just under a minute more, and I’ll be fully recovered.’ Yae-hime assumed a battle stance, silently calculating the time in her heart.

“Haah!” On the other side, Lucky let out a thunderous shout. His overwhelming aura surged behind him, condensing into a vague phantom. It was the form of a fearsome demon!

The crowd broke into uproar once again, and the audience watching the livestream were equally shaken.

“Your life is mine!” With his preparation complete, Lucky charged forth. His fierce aura tore a deep scar across the plaza as stone dust scattered into the air.

Knowing the opponent was about to go all out, Yae-hime’s mind grew taut, her eyes locked forward.

If Lucky had been like a 107mm shell before, he was now a guided missile! In the blink of an eye, the raging Lucky appeared before Yae-hime. His left hand transformed into a tiger’s claw, while his right hand took the form of a crane’s beak.

Behind him, the phantom shifted into the shapes of a fierce tiger and a celestial crane.

‘Tiger-Crane Double Form Fist?!’

Yae-hime had only grasped nine apertures of boxing arts, still far from true mastery. Naturally, she could not recognize exactly what technique he was using. All she could do was make a rough guess from his stance.

Lucky’s strike was blindingly swift, the tiger’s claw lunging directly for Yae-hime’s chest. At first glance, the move looked crude and underhanded. In truth, it really was underhanded.

Traditional martial arts and modern combat techniques were two completely different things. The latter had been stripped of too much substance, leaving little more than fitness routines and showy poses. The former was a true art of killing, aimed directly at the vulnerable points of the human body. Once it landed, it often meant instant death!

This was real combat, not some childish sporting match!

Yae-hime decisively tapped the ground with her toes and leapt backward, retreating to avoid the brunt of the strike. Her goal was clear—to buy time! Rather than waste strength trading blow for blow with Lucky, it was better to hold out until she recovered and then finish him with a single decisive strike!

But Lucky was not about to let her off easily. He stepped forward and darted after her, his fingers pinched together like the beak of a crane, stabbing ferociously toward Yae-hime’s temple.

She quickly steadied her stance, extending her slender hand just as before, trying to knock his strike aside. Only this time, it felt like striking against a block of solid iron, her force simply would not break through. Worse still, an overwhelming power pressed down upon her, shattering her defense.

The crane’s beak was about to pierce Yae-hime’s skull. But at that very moment, a translucent fox tail suddenly shot out, thrusting straight at Lucky’s heart. It carried the intent to pierce both his body and heart in one savage strike!

Sensing the deadly threat, Lucky immediately withdrew his hand, twisting his body sharply. At the very brink of disaster, he barely evaded the fox tail’s assassination attempt.

He spun once more to widen the distance. When his gaze returned to Yae-hime, she was already clad in a shimmering fox pelt, nine tails dancing joyfully around her.

“If you’re so eager to die, then I’ll be glad to play with you.”

+++

# **715 – Violent Duel, Evenly Matched?!**

Seeing Yae-hime with that fox tail manifested, the expressions of the audience instantly changed. There was both shock and admiration. The swaying fox tail, paired with her classical robes and peerless beauty, made her seem like Daji[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-113141) reborn.

“Sis, you look as beautiful as a painting!” Mylene clasped her small hands before her chest and spoke in excitement.

“Ah~ this is my first time seeing Princess in this form in reality. I’m in love, absolutely in love!” Pixie’s eyes grew hazy, her legs turned weak, and an unnatural flush spread across her face.

Several onlookers with weaker mental fortitude were instantly bewitched, their minds thrown into disarray. Even though the aura that Princess now exuded was no different from that of a god of slaughter, they still felt an urge to approach her, like moths drawn to a flame.

“Hey!” At that moment, a Grandmaster at the front let loose a thunderous shout, jolting everyone awake. “If you want to die, then step forward.” The Grandmaster’s expression was stern as he spoke.

Upon hearing this, those spectators who had taken steps forward shuddered in horror, their hearts chilled.

“Fox… fox spirit!” someone cried out in terror.

“This woman carries a demonic allure!”

“Yes, yes, just now it was like I was under a spell!”

“She’s a calamity incarnate!”

“Far too terrifying!”

The audience members who had retreated back to their places were left shaken and full of lingering fear. If they had rushed into the battle between two Grandmasters, it would have ended in a bloodbath. Those with weaker strength would have been torn to shreds in an instant.

Lucky stared fixedly at Yae-hime. His face remained calm, but inwardly he was shaken. This young Grandmaster was clearly far stronger than the usual Primary Grandmaster. That last exchange had given him the illusion of brushing death itself. It felt as though, had he been half a beat slower, his body would have been completely pierced through by that fox tail.

Yae-hime wore a calm expression, but inside she was irritated. She had originally planned to toy with Lucky casually until her body fully recovered, then take him down in a single blow to shock the entire audience.

‘Some Grandmasters among the spectators are releasing hostile auras. They seem to be my enemies.’

Her intent in intimidating the crowd was not out of vanity. She wanted to warn those Grandmasters not to make a move against her. Otherwise, she would show no mercy. To achieve such an effect, she had to defeat Lucky in a single strike.

If she became entangled with him for too long, complications would inevitably arise. After all, there were too many Grandmasters and transcendents present. Who could say whether they would all suddenly turn on her?

If that happened, she and her allies would be forced into a passive situation. Such an outcome was the last thing Yae-hime wanted to see.

However, Lucky’s opening strike had been so vicious that she was left with no choice but to delay her recovery and clash head-on with him.

‘The final strike will be the key.’ Since she could no longer follow her original plan, she could only adapt as the battle unfolded. Yae-hime steadied her heart, her expression gradually turning serious.

The two of them locked eyes, neither making the next move.

Lucky remained filled with caution. Although he had great confidence in himself, the strength this opponent displayed was far from ordinary. He had to tread carefully. Otherwise, if he capsized in such a shallow gutter, it would not be fun at all.

‘Even if there is only a one percent chance of that happening, I will never allow it!’ Lucky was both confident and cautious.

As the two stared each other down, the atmosphere grew unnaturally oppressive. Even though neither had moved, the collision of their fierce auras alone exerted an indescribable pressure on everyone present.

**Tap!**

Suddenly, the quiet square echoed with the sound of a footstep. In the next instant, Yae-hime shot forward. This time, she intended to strike first!

Lucky’s eyes sharpened, his expression shifting abruptly as though facing a mortal threat. In that very moment, he treated Yae-hime as a powerful enemy worthy of his full strength. If necessary, he was even prepared to unleash his strongest means to kill her outright.

With a swish, Yae-hime unfurled all nine tails at once, launching a storm-like assault. The way she moved, it seemed as if she intended to beat Lucky to death in an instant.

But Lucky was no weakling. As the fox tails came whipping toward him at terrifying speed, he let out a thunderous shout. From behind him, a shadowy specter surged forth, unleashing a furious Tiger-Crane dance!

The clash of their forces detonated into deafening roars.

**Crack!**

The ground could not withstand the level of their power. The heavy stone tiles split apart at frightening speed. From their center, a web of fractures spread outward like a spider’s web.

Witnessing such a terrifying exchange, most of the spectators stood dumbfounded, their hearts shaken to the core. This battle had already gone far beyond the scope of human understanding. It was as though two humanoid monsters were locked in a frenzy of slaughter!

Thrilling—this was no ordinary thrill! Many spectators felt their very blood boil, an inexplicable blaze igniting in their hearts.

Far away in the United States, Mira was also watching the live broadcast, her face etched with undisguised shock. She had truly not expected that Princess would remain so overwhelmingly powerful in the real world!

No, to be precise, she was still somewhat weaker. After all, she carried no equipment, nor did she have any attribute boosts. But even so, as a Grandmaster, her strength was simply outrageous.

“My God, her danger rating ought to be raised yet again!”

A Primary Grandmaster and an Intermediate Grandmaster fighting to a standstill, how could she not be shaken? At this point, even if Mira switched places with Lucky, she would have no absolute confidence in defeating her opponent.

Ronald was also watching this duel, his shock no less than Mira’s. No, in truth, his shock climbed to an even greater height. After all, when they had first met, Princess had only been at the Master level. Compared to now, the difference was like heaven and earth.

“Terrifying… this girl is simply too terrifying!” Staring at the broadcast, Ronald’s entire body trembled, and even his voice quavered when he spoke.

When he first heard that Princess had already reached the Grandmaster level, he had been stunned for a long time before calming down.

While sighing at how the new generation always surpasses the old, he also felt a trace of relief. But now, seeing Princess evenly matched against Lucky, who had advanced to the Intermediate Grandmaster stage, his heart was filled with horror.

What kind of monster was this!? Recalling the moment when he had once suppressed her, Ronald felt as though it had been nothing but a dream. It did not feel real in the slightest.

Clearly, only a short time had passed. Yes, precisely because so little time had passed, it all felt especially unreal.

“…” Fixing his gaze on the broadcast, he remained lost in thought for a long while.

---

Back on the plaza.

Yae-hime and Lucky clashed with fists and feet, their violent exchange unleashing shockwaves that shattered the surrounding ground, hurling rubble into the air and raising clouds of dust.

Such a breathtaking battle left the crowd both enthralled and shaken to the core.

Moments ago, a brick-sized piece of debris had shot past overhead like a cannonball. Had it struck someone head-on, they would have been killed instantly! Fortunately, the powerful experts at the very front had blocked most of the dangers for them.

That particular stone had simply flown too high, slipping through the net. And thankfully, it caused no injuries.

**Boom!**

Suddenly, a deafening blast erupted. Yae-hime and Lucky’s fists collided with brutal force, the mighty impact bursting outward from them in concentric shockwaves!

#### **Footnotes:**

1. Refers to a legendary nine-tailed fox spirit from ancient China, who was the favorite consort of King Zhou, the last ruler of the Shang dynasty.

+++

# **716 – Countdown to Power Recovery**

“Waaah!” Even though the spectators were standing at a fair distance, the rapidly spreading shockwave still sent many of them staggering, tumbling left and right, screams breaking out all around.

But their ordeal was far from over. A thunderous boom resounded again as a second shockwave erupted. The ground cracked apart with a deafening roar, countless fragments shooting outward in all directions.

It was like being swept by a machine gun barrage! A single strike from those shards would not only maim but could easily kill. In an instant, raw terror surged up from the depths of the crowd’s hearts, spreading across their faces in waves of dread.

Just as despair was about to take hold, the Grandmasters and S-class transcendents at the front finally made their move. Their surging auras instantly solidified into barriers, blocking every fragment that came hurtling toward the crowd.

Yet the assault did not end there. A deafening rumble followed. The center of the square split apart, jagged fissures tearing open across the stone. Moments later, two figures were blasted from the cloud of dust, sent flying backward as the fiercest shockwave yet ripped outward.

Debris exploded into the air, sand and dust engulfing the sky.

The gathered powerhouses had no choice but to get serious, bracing themselves against the third impact. Seeing this, Pixie also stepped in to defend. Mylene tried to join her, but was quickly stopped.

“Right now, many factions still don’t know you exist. There’s no need to reveal yourself.”

Hearing this, Mylene nodded and decisively withdrew to the side.

This new shockwave came raging in, carrying the weight of ten thousand tons. Had it struck the weaker ones in the crowd, the result would have been nothing short of a human catastrophe.

Such was the destructive power of Grandmaster-level combat, terrifying beyond belief.

Thanks to the shielding of the experts, the audience behind them narrowly escaped disaster. Most only suffered scrapes or bruises from being knocked about. Yet the survivors felt as though they had just clawed their way back from the gates of death, their hearts pounding wildly in their chests.

It was thrilling, yet utterly terrifying. Those watching the live broadcast felt their scalps tingle, their bodies trembling with excitement. Some even screamed aloud, nearly fainting on the spot.

A battle that surpassed human limits, it made blood surge through the veins, igniting exhilaration beyond control!

A gust of sea breeze swept through, blowing away the lingering dust and revealing two figures. On the left stood a maiden like an immortal descended from the ninth heaven. On the right stood a middle-aged man, his face slightly pale.

Both stood tall and unyielding, their bodies radiating an oppressive aura that sent shivers down spines. The watching elites couldn’t conceal their astonishment as they looked upon the standoff.

That man, Lucky, was even stronger than they had imagined! But what shocked them even more was Yae-hime. A Primary Grandmaster, yet she was actually holding her ground against an Intermediate Grandmaster.

‘I knew I wasn’t mistaken last time… Princess truly is stronger than me.’ Pixie herself was shaken. At best, her strength could allow her to fight Lucky to a draw. On the surface, the two combatants had seemed evenly matched. But Pixie could clearly see the difference in their auras.

Lucky was already beginning to falter. Meanwhile, Princess’ aura only grew more intense with every passing moment. And to think, she had entered this fight already wounded!

Returning to her place, Pixie glanced at Mylene and softly asked, “Just what realm is your sister at now?”

Mylene shook her head. The shock she felt was no less than Pixie’s. Her sister’s strength was like an unfathomable abyss, there was no finding the bottom.

Watching the live broadcast, Ronald sat utterly stunned. Lucky’s power alone was enough to leave him deeply shaken. This man, whom Ronald had nearly erased from memory, had in the end surpassed him.

Yet even that shock was nothing compared to the awe Princess inspired. And to what extent? As though she towered above them like a figure three or four stories high.

“What kind of monster is this…” Suddenly, Ronald recalled that mysterious Kun Ruins. Only those prodigies who came from there could shine with such brilliance!

---

In Yanjing, at the Ye family estate. Donald was also watching the broadcast, his face showing a trace of shock, though not excessively. “So this is the strength of a genius from Kun Ruins… truly terrifying!”

At the same time, inside the Mo family tower. Lisa said nothing, though her eyes gleamed with admiration. ‘If I remember correctly, Princess had only just stepped into the Grandmaster Realm not long ago.’

“To clash head-on with an Intermediate level Grandmaster as a mere Primary, and even gain the upper hand. That kind of talent is only slightly beneath mine.” Lisa let out a calm smile, feeling her decision to win her over from the very beginning had been absolutely correct.

Back at the plaza. Lucky’s eyes locked on Yae-hime, his clenched fists creaking audibly. It was as if he wanted to crush the shock and dread within his heart to pieces.

‘Why is this woman growing stronger with every exchange!?’ At the start, he had managed to press a slight advantage. But with that last punch, Lucky realized something was wrong. Her strike had actually been stronger than his own!

‘For someone so young to already wield such strength… her future is unimaginable. No! I must kill her as soon as possible!’ At that moment, the killing intent in Lucky’s heart surged higher than ever, a cold light flashing in his eyes.

Across from him, Yae-hime exhaled softly, a serene look appearing on her face. After such an intense clash, it was hardly surprising that her strength had not weakened but increased.

By using the Green Emperor’s Longevity Art in combat, her mana consumption naturally increased. Still, the faster her body healed, the sooner her strength returned. Her true power had always been far above Lucky’s.

Now, it was merely returning to its natural state.

“You have fifteen seconds left to pray to your god.” She pointed at Lucky, her voice calm and indifferent. The words sounded like a proclamation of victory. To others, it came across as unbearably arrogant. Yet Yae-hime had only spoken the truth.

“Fifteen seconds?” Grandmaster Kim of Korea allowed a faint smirk to curl at his lips, his expression mocking. In his view, Yae-hime was indeed powerful, but like many of the young, she was far too conceited.

Such arrogance, that dismissive contempt for all others, was not a virtue. One must remember, the foundation of veteran Grandmasters ran deep indeed!

“Still too young.” Grandmaster Ota shook his head lightly. Just moments ago, he had held a favorable opinion of Yae-hime, but with those words, his impression of her dropped by half.

She had fallen into the very mistake that most young people inevitably made. That arrogance would eventually lead her straight to the underworld.

The experts present were all seasoned veterans, having seen far more of the world and eaten more salt than Yae-hime had eaten rice. At this moment, every one of them lost faith in her.

“Hahahahaha!” Suddenly, a wild burst of laughter rang out.

All turned toward the sound, only to see Lucky throwing his head back, laughing as though he had just heard the most ridiculous joke of his life, one so absurd it could split his sides.

Yet the laughter ended abruptly, cut off in an instant. Lucky closed his mouth and fixed his gaze on Yae-hime, his expression as frigid as winter. The killing intent within him had soared to its peak.

No—what also surged was a fury like a volcano on the verge of eruption. He felt that this insolent woman before him had gravely offended him. She had to die. Immediately.

“You have ten seconds left.” In response, Yae-hime remained utterly composed, as if she had never placed him in her eyes at all.

That unshaken demeanor sent Lucky’s rage and bloodlust bursting forth completely, spilling from his mouth. “Kill!”

+++

# **717 – Full Power Versus Full Power, A Frightening Revival**

The moment the word “kill” was uttered, nearly everyone felt a chill crawl down their spine. It was as if the temperature in the air had suddenly dropped by more than ten degrees.

Before the last syllable even faded, Lucky’s body began to undergo a startling transformation. Veins bulged across his forehead, and his muscles swelled rapidly, nearly tearing apart his bright yellow martial robe.

In an instant, his entire frame looked a full size larger than before. But it was not just his body that changed, his strength surged violently as well. A storm of violent energy burst out from within him, spreading outward and sending nearby debris flying into the air.

The ground trembled, and even space itself seemed to ripple faintly.

When his aura finally reached its peak, Lucky’s skin had turned a dark bronze, his pupils gleamed with a cold light, and an overwhelming, terrifying pressure radiated from his body.

This was his ultimate hidden technique—Bloodburning Art. An ancient forbidden spell once used by sorcerers of old. It drew power by burning one’s own vital blood essence, granting a temporary but tremendous boost in strength.

The cost, however, was severe…each use drastically reduced his ability to reproduce. Moreover, after the bloodburning subsided, the body would be left weakened for anywhere between a single day to ten.

Unless driven to desperation, he would never willingly reveal this card. Yet this was also the very ace that had allowed Lucky to return to Cathay and sweep across the whole world with unmatched dominance.

Only with such a trump card had he dared to flaunt his might upon his return.

“Th-this… this has to be a lie…” As he felt the aura radiating from Lucky, Grandmaster Ota’s eyes widened, his pupils contracted sharply, and disbelief spilled from his trembling lips. For the aura Lucky now radiated was unmistakably at the level of an Advanced Grandmaster!

“This man actually kept such a card hidden,” Pixie remarked in surprise. She faintly guessed that Lucky had used some kind of forbidden technique to reach such a state.

“It must come at some cost,” Mylene commented flatly, her tone calm and detached.

“You’re not worried about Princess?” Pixie turned to her and asked.

“Just look at her, does she look like someone who needs our worry?” Mylene gently shook her head.

Pixie glanced at Yae-hime, only to find that she too bore the same calm expression, as though she regarded Lucky’s temporary surge in strength as nothing worth mentioning.

‘Just how strong has Princess become?’ An irrepressible curiosity stirred within her heart.

Apart from Mylene and Pixie, every other expert present had their full attention locked on Lucky. It was as if they were seeing him for the very first time, their faces openly displayed shock, and even a trace of dread.

No one had expected Lucky to still be hiding such a terrifying trump card. Had they not witnessed it with their own eyes, none would have believed that someone could forcibly break through to a higher realm in such a manner.

The majority of those watching the live broadcast could only stare in vague awe, not truly understanding. Only a few managed to faintly perceive the truth. Yet, since they were not at the scene, they could not feel the sheer intensity of Lucky’s aura.

Otherwise, they too would have been stricken with fear and trembling.

“Two seconds have passed,” Yae-hime’s voice rang out just then. Her tone was calm and level, betraying not a single hint of fear or surprise.

Could it be that she felt no shock at all? That she did not find this terrifying in the slightest? Or perhaps, she simply did not realize just how overwhelming her opponent’s strength had become?

Grandmaster Ota sighed inwardly, as though he could already see the tragic scene of her death playing out before his eyes.

After his initial shock, Grandmaster Kim’s expression quickly returned to calm. He spoke softly, “A woman who cannot see the situation clearly, it is time for her to wither.”

“Oh, my Yahweh!” Thunder God Johnny stared fixedly at Lucky, every hair on his body standing on end as a tidal wave of shock crashed within him.

Just moments ago, he had believed himself to be the strongest one here. Who could have guessed that Lucky would suddenly transform into a hulking brute, his strength soaring to a level Johnny could no longer even hope to reach.

Truly, there was always a higher sky, always someone stronger beyond oneself!

“Three seconds.” As though oblivious to the situation and blind to her opponent’s newfound power, Yae-hime continued her leisurely count.

“Scared stiff already?” Lucky turned toward her, the corners of his mouth curling upward. “Didn’t you say earlier that you’d give me fifteen seconds to pray? Heh, let’s see if you can even last fifteen seconds!”

The instant his words fell, Lucky vanished from sight. He appeared before Yae-hime like a phantom flash, and if not for the deafening boom that followed and the cloud of dust exploding behind him, the crowd would have believed he had truly teleported.

“Five.” Yae-hime remained unruffled even as she looked at the towering figure, now bulkier than before.

Such composure was deeply infuriating.

“Go to hell!” Having been ignored again and again, Lucky was now seething with rage. His strike came at full force. His fist, larger than an iron pot, shot forward, the gale it stirred so fierce it was visible to the naked eye. The destructive power was beyond imagination!

As the colossal fist closed in, reflected in her eyes, Yae-hime’s expression finally shifted. She seemed to become just a little more serious. Her toes tapped the ground, and she shot backward in retreat.

Lucky’s savage blow missed, yet the spiraling fist wind still howled toward her, chasing her down. That powerful gale swept up gravel and dust along its path, its destructive force multiplying.

If struck head-on, she would surely be battered and bloodied.

“Six.” Facing such a fierce torrent of force, Yae-hime quickly steadied her stance. With a graceful hand thrust forward, her aura surged outward, forming a barrier wall.

Almost simultaneously, the fist wind slammed into it with a thunderous boom. Dust and stone fragments blasted in every direction. The strike looked overwhelming, yet in truth, it did not injure Yae-hime in the slightest.

“Give me your life!” No—this had only been a feint. Lucky’s true killing move had just arrived. Out of the dust, a blurred figure streaked forth. One hand pierced through the energy wall, its five fingers forming a tiger’s claw that lunged straight for Yae-hime’s chest.

It was the same martial form, yet the power was entirely different. The onlookers felt as if they were witnessing a ravenous tiger pouncing upon a helpless little girl, ready to devour her whole.

“Seven.” Yet this _helpless girl_… no, Yae-hime, still did not treat Lucky as worthy of concern. She continued her count even as she stepped forward and threw a straight punch to meet his ambush head-on.

“Hah! You think too highly of yourself!” Lucky laughed in fury at her audacity, and his tiger claw swiped down with ferocity.

A muffled thud rang out. The next instant, a figure was hurled backward. It was Yae-hime. She had been struck by that ferocious claw and sent flying.

“Pathetic, not even worth a blow!” Having landed a solid strike, Lucky rushed after her without pause. His Bloodburning Art could only last for three minutes. Once that time was up, his body would weaken severely.

‘I must kill her quickly and return to the ship. If my weakness is exposed, it will put me at a disadvantage!’

“Nine.” Even as she flew back, Yae-hime did not forget to keep counting. Only one more second remained before her body fully recovered.

Lucky instantly closed the gap, his figure radiating both the shadows of tiger and crane, his momentum overwhelming.

‘This blow will decide everything!’ Though he had no idea that Yae-hime’s body was restoring itself, an unshakable premonition gnawed at his heart, warning him of grave danger. He had to kill her quickly!

“Ten. Your time has come, go report to the heavens!”

At the very moment Lucky struck, Yae-hime’s count concluded. A horrifying, monstrous aura erupted from her body, surging outward like a storm and stunning the entire battlefield!

+++

# **718 – Eat My Lightning Poison Dragon Drill!**

Death. In that instant, everyone felt an incomparably terrifying aura of death. It was as if their hearts had been seized in the crushing grip of death’s claws. As if their very souls were being cruelly hooked halfway out of their bodies. As if they would perish utterly in the next heartbeat.

It felt as though their very lives were being crushed in another’s grasp, leaving them in agony, suffocation, and helpless fear.

At that moment, whether warrior, transcendent, or ordinary person, all appeared no greater than ants, insignificant, pitiful, and powerless.

At the very heart of that aura stood Lucky, frozen in place like a fool. His complexion turned deathly pale, his features contorted, his eyes stretched wide, and his pupils contracted to pinpoints. Unlike those at a distance, he alone endured the full weight of this suffocating aura of death, and he felt its despair with terrifying clarity. It was as though his very heart had been encased in ice.

Lucky could scarcely believe what he was experiencing. It was like watching a Chihuahua suddenly morph into a Tyrannosaurus Rex before his very eyes.

Grotesque, horrifying beyond words. And now, that Tyrannosaurus was reaching out toward him. A hand as pale as jade, smooth and impossibly alluring.

In this strange realm where time itself seemed to have stopped, Yae-hime thrust out her palm.

Lucky stared at that palm without blinking. It was slow, unbearably, agonizingly slow. Like an ant crawling forward.

Against such an attack, he had ten thousand ways to deflect it, and fifteen thousand ways to counterattack. Yet the instant he tried to move, he realized his body could not budge at all. It was as if he had been bound by a paralyzing spell, unable even to twitch a finger.

That beautiful hand still pressed forward at its maddeningly slow pace. The slender, delicate fingers, the rosy whiteness of the palm, every detail was something one could not help but admire. But to Lucky, this palm was unspeakably horrifying, like the claw of a demon.

‘Move… move, damn it!’ He summoned every ounce of strength, but his body still refused to respond.

Something was terribly wrong.

Then, from the corner of his eye, he caught a glimpse of the distant spectators. They too were frozen in place, as if time had halted for them as well. Which meant, in this suspended world, only the girl before him was still moving!

That flawless palm drew closer, bringing with it a faint, fresh fragrance.

‘Don’t—don’t come any closer!’ Lucky screamed inwardly, his mind already drowned in terror. How he wished this was only a nightmare. If only he could open his eyes and wake, the nightmare would end, and everything would return to normal.

But unfortunately, this was reality.

At last, that jade-white hand pressed against Lucky’s chest. Whether he wanted it or not, that palm descended like an undeniable truth, flawless and unstoppable.

Immediately, the stagnant flow of time resumed. No, it was not time that had stopped. It was Lucky’s perception returning to normal. The strangeness he had just felt was not a true suspension of time, but the sheer speed of Yae-hime’s strike, which warped his senses into the illusion of slowness.

To the spectators, the moment Yae-hime released her aura, she had already launched a phantom-like counterattack. So fast that it was nearly invisible to the naked eye. Only a handful of the stronger ones in the crowd managed to glimpse the trajectory of her strike.

**Crack!**

A sharp sound rang out from Lucky’s chest. The sound of ribs shattering. The next instant, he felt as though he had been rammed by a runaway dump truck at full speed. Every ounce of air in his body was forced out, and an excruciating, heart-piercing pain erupted.

Then his body shot backward like a cannonball, the violent impact gouging a deep trench into the ground. In an instant, dirt and debris exploded into the air, scattering in every direction.

The scene fell into utter silence. People had only just shaken off the shadow of death, yet now they were witnessing such a ferocious assault that their hearts were caught between shock and fear.

This was especially true for the grandmasters and S-rank transcendents. When they looked at Lucky, who had been blasted away like a cannonball, it felt as though they were looking at themselves.

No, if it had been them dueling that humanoid monster, they would likely have fallen fifteen seconds earlier.

Mylene and Pixie both revealed expressions of astonishment. It was clear that Yae-hime’s strength had already surpassed anything they could have imagined.

“Big Sister is incredible!” Mylene cried out in excitement.

“Yes… but where did Princess go?” Pixie was about to nod in agreement when she suddenly realized that Yae-hime had vanished from sight.

“There!” Mylene’s eyes shifted, widening in surprise as she saw Yae-hime materialize behind Lucky like a phantom.

Everyone who witnessed this scene was dumbfounded, their hearts shaken to the core.

At that moment, Lucky spat out a mouthful of blood. Just as he tried to steady himself, he sensed an extremely dangerous aura right behind him. His heart trembled with dread as he attempted to twist his body and evade.

Unfortunately, it was already too late. Yae-hime’s right foot stepped forward, her body sliding to the left, as she suddenly unleashed an Iron Mountain Slam.[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116404)　

With a thunderous bang, Lucky took the blow head-on, his entire body convulsing as a tidal wave of force erupted outward. In that instant, he felt his bones shatter, his organs rupture, and his body churn as if it had been thrown into a blender. The agony was enough to make him feel both like dying and transcending.

The plaza, already broken and damaged, had yet another layer of stone peeled away by the impact of that shockwave. If even the aftermath was that terrifying, then for Lucky, who had taken the strike directly, the result could only be imagined.

Just like before, the burly grandmaster’s body shot through the air once again. A wretched scream tore from his throat, so shrill and piercing that it made everyone’s scalp prickle and their hearts quiver.

The man who only moments ago exuded invincible arrogance was now being battered without mercy, reduced to the state of a dead dog.

Terrifying…this Princess was terrifying beyond measure.

And it was not only Lucky’s body being hurled away that stunned the crowd. Yae-hime had already reappeared before him in a blur. She crouched low, one hand pressing firmly against the ground, then flickered into motion as her right leg shot upward in a rising kick that slammed squarely into Lucky’s chin.

In that instant, an illusion of his head being torn from his body filled his mind. His body shot upward like a skyrocketing firework.

But Yae-hime’s assault did not end there. She pivoted into a half-spin to regain her stance, stomped against the ground, and seemed to teleport into the air above him. If not for the sight of the ground beneath her cracking apart, many would have believed she had truly teleported.

High in the air. Yae-hime twisted her body mid-flight and unleashed a fierce inverted scissor kick, slamming it against Lucky’s undefended frame.

The pitiful man, who had only just been kicked skyward, had not even processed the pain before he was struck again and sent plummeting down. The momentum that carried him up now drove him down with equal ferocity.

**Boom!**

Lucky’s body fell from above like a five-ton air conditioner, crashing into the ground with an earth-shattering impact.

Above, Yae-hime hung suspended in mid-air, her aura erupting into violet lightning that crackled and hissed. Her gaze sharpened, and her body whirled like a spinning top before she plunged downward, transforming into a storm of violet thunder that crashed upon the earth with devastating force.

+++

# **719 – Humans Cannot Truly Understand One Another**

On the ground. Actually… by now, Lucky’s entire body had sunk into the earth, leaving him unable to move.

Watching that terrifying human-shaped storm descend, he could only let out a desperate wail. Unfortunately, his cry of despair was immediately drowned out by a thunderous roar.

**Boom!**

The moment Yae-hime’s foot slammed down, the ground erupted and a violent tremor spread outward. In the next instant, a terrifying shockwave rippled out in expanding circles, surging farther and farther.

The battlefield was torn by raging winds, as if a natural disaster had descended upon them. At once, the stronger fighters again stepped forward as shields for the crowd. This time, however, they struggled bitterly to withstand the force.

If the previous aftershocks had been like a drizzle, then now they were a storm unleashed! The viewers watching the livestream were nearly dumbstruck as one.

Such a cataclysmic strike, yet it came from a human hand, how could anyone believe it? Some even suspected it might be computer-generated effects, a trick to scam money. But when they recalled the reputation of the consortium behind it, they had no choice but to dismiss the thought.

“Oh my Yahweh… no, wait, I don’t even follow a religion!” Vera gasped at the broadcast screen. She had been too busy until now to watch the fight. Yet less than ten seconds in, Yae-hime’s terrifying power had completely silenced her.

Seeing this devastating strike, her heart trembled uncontrollably. Just what kind of monster had she been trying to oppose all this time?

“M-maybe I’d better not trouble her again.” Vera’s fire for revenge was instantly extinguished. Little did she know that a place in Yae-hime’s City of Chaos had already been reserved for her. Whether sooner or later, being captured and made to work was inevitable.

* **Roc City, Abilities Management Bureau.**

“Monster…” Ronald’s body shook violently, barely managing to utter the word.

* **Yanjing, Mo family’s Mansion.**

“Hmph… hmph, this level of talent is only a step beneath my own!” Lisa muttered, her eye twitching, face faintly red.

At this moment, all the magnates following the battle wore expressions of awe, their hearts shaken to the core. An eighteen-year-old grandmaster whose power reached such terrifying heights, this was no blessing to them. It was a threat. A tremendous threat that had to be destroyed swiftly. Otherwise, once the youth fully matured, where would they find a foothold in this world?

Yae-hime could never have imagined that unleashing her full strength merely to intimidate those who sought trouble… Would instead earn her the hostility of countless powerful figures.

* **America, Dorado.**

Mira suddenly received a message that snapped her out of her shock.

“As expected, you’ve reached SS-rank. From now on, Princess, life won’t be so easy for you.” Mira’s lips curved into a faint smile. A flame blazed in her chest, and a spark of battle-lust flashed in her eyes.

* **Back at the battlefield.**

The disaster-like strike finally subsided, its aftershocks completely dispersed.

The sea breeze swept away the clouds of dust, revealing a vast black conical crater. At its center stood a stunning figure. Who else could it be but Yae-hime, beautiful beyond compare, a vision of celestial grace descended upon the mortal world?

At her feet, Lucky lay in a pool of blood, eyes rolled back, his body broken and mangled. Whether he still lived was unclear.

Silence reigned over the scene. No one dared to speak. Not even the slightest movement was made. They feared even the smallest noise might provoke a reaction from that monster.

“This square doesn’t have a name yet, does it?” Suddenly, Yae-hime withdrew her slender leg from Lucky’s body, turned, and slowly lifted her gaze toward the onlookers, asking in a detached tone.

Though some distance separated them, the audience heard her words with startling clarity.

She walked forward step by step, awaiting their answer. Yet no one at the scene uttered a word. It wasn’t that they were afraid to reply. They truly didn’t know! A temporary plaza hastily constructed, what need was there for a name?

“Don’t know? Very well.” Yae-hime stepped out of the crater, her aura extending into countless tendrils that suddenly lashed at the ground.

Fragments of earth and soil burst into the air.

Her abrupt action left everyone staring in bewilderment. After a few seconds, Yae-hime finally stopped. Her aura spread outward again, scattering the dust.

“From now on, this place shall be called Yae-hime Square.” She glanced at the crowd, speaking casually. As soon as her words fell, the audience saw a few large characters appear on the ground.

**Yae-hime**

In an instant, someone realized that this was Princess’ true name. She was declaring her real name to the world!

With tonight’s earth-shaking battle, she engraved her name upon this square, leaving an indelible mark on the hearts of all. At once, the name “Yae-hime” began to echo across the globe.

From this moment onward, Yaeger’s female identity finally broke free from the title of Princess…

“Princess!” Just then, Pixie and Mylene came running over, the former happily calling out her _name_. It seemed that shedding that title was still too soon.

“I made you worry.” Yae-hime smiled.

“That was truly a spectacular fight. I was so excited, I nearly got wet—ah, I mean, I was so fired up just watching!” Pixie paused mid-sentence, awkwardly changing her words.

“Sis, you were so amazing!” Mylene threw herself onto Yae-hime’s arm, speaking with bubbling excitement.

Beside her, Pixie’s heart was full of envy. She, too, wanted to cling to Yae-hime’ other arm. But she feared Yae-hime might not like it.

‘Ahh, if only I were Mylene!’ For now, she could only watch with envy, drooling inwardly.

Yae-hime chatted with them briefly before turning her gaze toward the assembled powerhouses. From earlier, she had already sensed a few hostile auras lingering among them.

“Does anyone else wish to challenge me?” Yae-hime’s voice was cold. Her words plunged the square into dead silence.

At this point, who would be stupid enough to provoke a monster like her? Were they so eager to die?

Grandmaster Kim from Korea clenched his fists. His face remained calm, but inside he seethed with humiliation and fury. His disciple had been slaughtered by this monster, yet he had no power to seek justice. The frustration was unbearable.

Several other experts felt the same suffocating anger. She had openly provoked them, and yet none dared to step forward. Their chests burned with shame.

Of course, they could force themselves into battle. But that would only mean courting humiliation. Even Lucky, who had broken through temporarily, had been crushed. Who else among them qualified to fight her?

None. Not a single one.

What made them despair even more was that this monster’s aura still surged with terrifying strength! Trying to take advantage now was nothing but a fool’s dream.

Grandmaster Ota stared at Yae-hime, the shock on his face still lingering. An eighteen-year-old grandmaster, emerging like a blazing star, the impact on the martial world would be unprecedented.

‘Good thing I hedged my bet. Otherwise, I’d have taken a huge loss tonight!’ Suddenly recalling his wager, he felt a secret flicker of joy.

Knowing she had already cowed them, Yae-hime withdrew her gaze and turned to her two companions. “It’s getting late. Let’s go back. Since my transport was destroyed on the way, I’ll trouble you for a ride on your ship.”

At her words, Pixie immediately slipped her arm around Yae-hime’s. “Of course, Princess! Mylene, let’s go home!”

Mylene rolled her eyes, inwardly marveling at her companion’s ability to seize every opportunity.

Only after they left the square did the rest of the crowd finally exhale in relief. What followed was a chaos of emotions, some felt empty, some thrilled, others seethed with rage.

The plaza buzzed with an uproarious mix of reactions.

+++

# **720 – Aftershocks and a Subtle Sense of Familiarity**

In the pitch-black ocean, the fisheries patrol vessel No. 2105 sped swiftly toward Roc City’s harbor.

Inside the cabin, Yae-hime, Pixie, and Mylene sat together on the sofa. To be precise, Yae-hime was lying with her head pillowed on Mylene’s lap, while her own legs rested across Pixie’s thighs.

As for how things had turned out this way, the story was long enough to fill a roll of cloth. Long story short… she was simply too popular.

At that moment, Yae-hime had already entered the game. It was her first time letting herself appear so defenseless before others. Well, strictly speaking, Pixie and Mylene could hardly be called outsiders.

One was her own little sister. The other was her confidante from the past life. That was why she could lower her guard and enter the game without worry.

“These legs… I could play with them forever…” Pixie’s cheeks were flushed, her beautiful eyes fixed unblinkingly on Yae-hime’s flawless legs as she whispered under her breath.

Mylene faintly caught her words and turned her head with a puzzled look.
