# **738 – Your Delusions, I’ll Be the One to Shatter Them.**

Going back a little in time…

Jade City remained as lively as ever, though today’s bustle differed noticeably from usual. Whether guards or players, everyone’s eyes carried obvious streaks of red.

The former had been ordered to hunt down that detestable Black-Hearted Princess and had not slept a wink. Most of the latter had spent the entire night searching for S.K.Y., and only a small minority were looking for the Black-Hearted Princess.

These players were not far from being forcibly logged out. They were filled with a stubborn unwillingness, convinced that with just a few more hours, they might actually find S.K.Y.

Right now, S.K.Y. was like Yae-hime in the past, someone everyone wanted a piece of. The difference was that after the battle in the Mangrove Forest, the vast majority of players had become utterly terrified of her.

Before they grew stronger, they did not even dare entertain a single improper thought. Of course, there were still a few naive dreamers clinging to blind hope. After all, dreams were free. What if one of them actually came true?

NightOut[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119677) sat by the window of a snack shop, cracking melon seeds while scrolling through game news, appearing completely relaxed.

In truth, he was a casual player who had little interest in leveling or equipment. NightOut came from Novice Village 101. He once partied with Little Fairy and had long witnessed the terror that was the Black-Hearted Princess. Naturally, he had no desire to “pluck her peach.”

Players who still harbored that kind of delusion were, in his eyes, definitely out of their minds.

“Huh? Did my eyes blur?” he muttered as he suddenly stared at the floating Level Ranking List. His expression shifted from calm to stunned, his eyes widening abruptly as his jaw dropped wide enough to fit a whole fist.

“F-forty… Forty!?” At last, the shock and disbelief exploding inside him burst out like a crack of spring thunder, startling everyone in the shop.

The locals immediately began shouting curses, and among the players, some scolded him while others sensed something amiss. Just now, this guy had shouted “forty!” Could a new World Boss have appeared?

None of them connected it to a player’s level, because until now, the highest level belonged only to the Black-Hearted Princes, who’s at Level 30. You ate your meal one bite at a time, after all. Even if that Black-Hearted Princess was practically a walking cheat engine, she couldn’t have suddenly jumped ten levels.

It had to be a new World Boss. That was what the players firmly believed. To them, while a World Boss wasn’t as enticing as the artifact on S.K.Y., it was still a delicious chunk of meat.

Who wouldn’t want a bite? If they got lucky and an Epic-grade item dropped, they would strike it rich! In an instant, many players imagined themselves bathing in a tub filled with money. It was utter bliss.

Unfortunately, beautiful fantasies remained nothing more than fantasies. At that moment, NightOut struck without mercy and shattered their delusions, “Heaven above! The Black-Hearted Princess hit Level 40!”

His voice spread like a scream straining to tear open his throat, stunning not only everyone inside but also frightening those outside. The locals were baffled. They only heard the words “Black-Hearted Princess,” yet even that alone struck them like thunder.

That imperial scourge, had she committed some new atrocity again? Otherwise, why would this outsider be so shocked?

The players felt their minds blank for a moment, and when they recovered, the expressions on their faces were a spectacle. Astonishment, disbelief, suspicion, dull confusion, silent shock, slack-jawed stares, furrowed brows, alarm… it was all there.

“That has to be a joke, right?” someone finally spoke, breaking the heavy silence.

“Of course it’s a joke. People nowadays don’t even need a picture in their posts to fool a whole bunch of idiots. They just want attention…disgusting!”

“Exactly! I checked the Black-Hearted Princess’ level one minute ago. Still Level 30, not even one level higher!” A Level 20 warrior spoke with absolute confidence.

“I checked thirty seconds ago. Also Level 30. This is confirmed rumor-mongering!”

“Do they really take us for fools?”

“Hmph, the face of someone whose lies get exposed is always so ugly.”

“A clown trying to stir up the crowd.”

The players in the shop all pointed fingers at NightOut, making his anger surge.

He was about to show them the proof when someone suddenly gasped, “Damn! She really hit Level 40!”

Everyone turned toward the voice. The player who had confidently claimed he checked the ranking thirty seconds earlier now stood pale-faced, staring at the leaderboard with a twisted expression.

A curious onlooker leaned over, catching a full, unobstructed view of the Level Ranking List. At the very top, the entry “Princess” stood out strikingly. The moment he looked at the level displayed, his eyes nearly popped out of their sockets. It unmistakably showed Level 40.

Seeing his distorted reaction, the surrounding players felt a sudden surge of doubt. Could it… actually be real? One after another, they opened the ranking list with skeptical hesitance.

Within two seconds, sharp gasps sounded repeatedly throughout the shop. The sudden chorus of cold inhalations made the temperature in the room feel as though it had dropped by ten degrees. Then came the outcry, an uproar that shook the entire space.

Watching the crowd’s nearly contorted expressions, NightOut flicked aside his dark bangs and let a mocking smile curl at the edge of his lips. “Got your faces slapped, didn’t you? Hurts, right?” he shouted.

Upon hearing this, the players’ expressions grew even uglier. They had just been loudly accusing him of fabricating nonsense, yet now the ranking list had smacked them square in the face. The embarrassment was unbearable.

The thin-skinned turned beet red. The thick-skinned said nothing and simply pretended to admire the scenery. Still, more than hurt pride, what bothered the players most was the leaderboard itself.

Jumping from Level 30 to Level 40, no matter how they looked at it, something had to be wrong with the ranking. It had to be a system error.

Someone quickly opened the forums and posted a question in the admin section, hoping for clarification. He expected no reply anytime soon. But this time, a response came instantly.

“Negative.” That was the administrator’s answer.

“It’s not a system bug!” the player shouted in shock. His voice instantly drew the attention of all nearby players. But to the natives, this outsider was merely yelling strange, incomprehensible syllables. It was unsettling.

Those who had firmly believed it was a system bug felt themselves slapped a second time. At this point, however, the embarrassment hardly mattered. What mattered was that, if it wasn’t a system bug, then the Black-Hearted Princess truly was Level 40.

How were they supposed to accept that?!

They rushed forward to confirm for themselves, and the truth staring back at them was more real than any pearl.

In the next moment, the entire shop fell into dead silence. Sensing the eerie quiet, the natives felt chills crawl up their spines. These outsiders were extremely strange. Before they could even grow properly frightened, a deafening chorus of shouts erupted.

“Cheating! This is blatant cheating!”

“The Black-Hearted Princess caught cheating red-handed!”

“What the hell! Wasn’t the level cap still 30?! Jumping straight to 40? That’s some outrageous cheating!”

“No wonder she’s so strong. Of course she was cheating!”

“Damn that cheater!”

“I refuse to accept this!”

The players inside the shop gradually lost control of their emotions. And it didn’t take long for that emotional chaos to spread through the forums… Eventually sweeping across the entire world.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. Syl: A casual player who’s ID is previously translated as “Not Returning Home Tonight (今夜不归家)”. I haven’t gone out of my way to edit his name in the past translations yet, not unless he turns out to be an important character…

+++

# **739 – Right Then, a Bunch of Sour Lemons Passed By**

In reality, Mira stared at the latest intel with both shock and disbelief written across her face. Although the Black-hearted Princess always seemed suspiciously like someone running cheats, she would never be stupid enough to use them so openly.

Besides, with her strength, she did not even need to raise her level to easily crush the global player base. So why bother doing something so pointless and expose herself?

The fact that the other party suddenly shot up ten levels made Mira feel that something was definitely off.

“Could she have triggered some sort of special mechanism?” Based on the intelligence Mira had gathered, there were indeed people who gained benefits through certain special mechanics in the game.

She herself had obtained quite a few benefits that way. That was exactly what an intelligence agency was for.

“No matter what, I need to push harder, or I’ll be left far, far behind!” Thinking about how she was only level 29 gave Mira a headache.

At this moment, not many people were thinking along the same lines as Mira. Most of the mainstream players, along with some who simply enjoyed watching drama, had been doubting since launch that the Black-hearted Princess only achieved her power through cheating.

And now, they finally had ‘solid proof.’

The moment Rakshasa logged in, she was immediately pulled into a chatroom. Naturally, the topic was this incident.

Nangong Lin: These people are literally jealous to the extreme.

Mylene: Right? Big Sis saved so much EXP. Once she broke through the zone’s level cap, getting to level forty isn’t strange at all.

Sachiel: So many sour little lemon spirits.

Little Fairy: If Princess were really using cheats, a single stomp from her would probably reduce them to dust.

Yunuen: Where do you even buy cheats for this game? I urgently need one!

Pixie: I don’t think this game could possibly have cheats.

Rakshasa: Hehe.

Nangong Lin: What are you laughing at?

Rakshasa: Secret.

Sachiel: Rakshasa, you’re so mean. You spark our curiosity and then refuse to say anything!

Yunuen: If I remember correctly, Rakshasa and Princess were both beta testers. Don’t tell me there’s really something hidden?

Rakshasa: I’m not telling you. That’s something between me and Princess~

Pixie: Wait…don’t tell me there really is a cheat?

Little Fairy: Shocked!

Rakshasa: No. We beta testers just had a slight advantage in the Novice Village, that’s all.

Nangong Lin: True. Twenty-four hours of beta testing wasn’t even enough to do anything.

Yunuen: …

Rakshasa: …

Nangong Lin: Why aren’t you two talking?

Sachiel: Auntie, did you forget everything Princess did in the Novice Village?

Nangong Lin: …Ahahaha, I almost forgot. My mind is full of all the wonderful memories I made with Princess.

Awww, how I wish to join up with Princess soon!

---

When those words came out, everyone except Yunuen and Little Fairy felt the same way.

Right after that, their conversation shifted to the progress of their various quests, and the matter of Yae-hime supposedly cheating was promptly thrown to the back of their minds.

On the Linhnan server’s forum, there were at least eight to ten thousand posts condemning the Black-hearted Princess. Each one read like the rant of a resentful woman.

And among them, jealous “lemon spirits” were practically everywhere. Posts like “Give me cheats and I’ll be number one too” alone numbered in the thousands. That sour, acidic smell practically seeped through the virtual screen.

Of course, there were also posts defending Yae-hime, but they were immediately drowned out by mobs of users. Labels like “paid shills,” “fifty-cent posters,” and “bootlickers” were slapped onto them without mercy.

Soon enough, posts of that sort vanished in the endless sea of threads. Even some well-reasoned analytical posts were accused of being attempts to “whitewash” her.

More often than not, people carried their own biases and only believed the version of events they wanted to believe, not the real truth. And once something contradicted their preconceived notions, they would erupt and attack as a group.

This phenomenon was widespread on the internet, and naturally it remained the same within the game. Strangely enough, while players all over the world were making a fuss, the system released no announcements at all. Not even a single notification chime.

Anyone with launch-day experience knew that the beta-tester incident had caused a massive uproar too. And in the end, everyone had benefited from it. So among the players stirring up noise now, a portion of them were doing it for the rewards.

As for the cheating accusations, they would sooner believe in ghosts. After all, this game was backed by the Five Great Nations, who would dare cheat, and who could even cheat?

Compared to the brainless majority, these players viewed the situation more calmly and simply hoped they could obtain some perks out of the commotion. However, their hopes were dashed. The system did not respond to them at all.

They were disappointed, so disappointed that it went far beyond anything ordinary. Some initiators suggested making an even bigger fuss. Unfortunately, not many people supported it. After all, pushing things too far would only cause trouble. And who among normal people wanted to wade into such muddy waters?

Even so, without anyone deliberately fanning the flames, the heat of the incident continued to rise. Before long, news outlets across the world were plastered with headlines about a cute gamer girl suspected of cheating.

Yae-hime knew none of this. And even if she had known, she would not have bothered to care. If people wanted to be sour, what could she do, refuse to let them be sour?

In truth, she really had activated a “future cheat.” But it was something she had traded her life to obtain. For every gain, there must be a loss. Besides, she was barely holding onto her male body as it was.

At this moment, Alicia had already dressed and was sitting on the bed, while Lili and Yae-hime sat on the chairs opposite her. Yae-hime sat on the chair; Lili sat on her lap, leaning her back against her breasts.

No, more accurately, her head was resting on it. Since she did not have her own, she was content to experience someone else’s. A faint curve lifted the corner of Lili’s lips.

After a brief cooldown period, both her and Alicia’s emotions had calmed. As though nothing had happened at all. But if one looked closely at their eyes, they would notice an unnatural redness lingering there.

“I don’t really know what to say, but…,” Alicia finally broke the silence. “This time, I truly owe you. Without you, I would’ve died.”

She knew very well what state her body had been in before she lost consciousness. It had been pushed to its absolute limit. If she had not managed to purge the earth energy from her body, even if she were revived, she would have ended up a cripple. She certainly would not be sitting here speaking like this.

“Why are you being so polite? Your problems are my problems,” Yae-hime replied with a calm smile.

Hearing that, Alicia froze for a moment before smiling back. “I suppose I was being a little too formal. Prin—right, I’ve always wanted to know your real name. Can you tell me now?”

At those words, Lili lifted her head to look up at Yae-hime, her face filled with curiosity.

“Yae-hime.” If this had been earlier, Yae-hime would not even have known how to answer. After all, back then, her female form had not even had a name.

“Yae-hime… it’s a lovely name. It suits you perfectly,” Alicia said with a gentle smile.

“Yae-hime… then I’ll call you Little Hime from now on,” Lili said cheerfully, leaning a bit more firmly against her breasts.

“As long as you’re happy,” Yae-hime replied helplessly. Why did everyone prefer to shorten her name? Was Yae-hime so hard to say?

“Little Hime.”

“I’m here.”

“Little Hime.”

“Yes.”

“Little Hime, Little Hime, Little Hime.”

“…” Yae-hime fell silent. This little brat was definitely playing around with her nickname!

“Back to the main topic. Alicia, I think the method you used to recover your strength has serious issues.” She shot Lili a glare, then turned to Alicia to steer the conversation back.

“Is there a problem? I just followed the method passed down by my ancestors,” Alicia said in confusion.

“Most of your ancestors were men, weren’t they? You know very well that men and women have very different bodies. What’s suitable for a man isn’t necessarily suitable for a woman. Your recovery method is far too rough. You need to be more delicate.” Yae-hime succinctly pointed out the core issue.

Hearing that, Alicia suddenly understood. “No wonder… If I hadn’t absorbed the earth energy so roughly, none of that would have happened!”

“It’ll be difficult for you to change your method right away. How about I help you instead?” Yae-hime offered the suggestion.

# **740 – I Know Your Body Better Than You Do**

“A-are you going to assist my recovery?” Alicia blinked, thinking she had misheard. After all, her strength had already recovered considerably, and the gap between her and Yae-hime had grown far greater than before.

Trying to fit a whole vat of water into a small cup simply wasn’t realistic. In Alicia’s mind, Yae-hime simply hadn’t realized how enormous the difference between them remained, which was why she said such a thing.

She appreciated the goodwill. But an impossible task would remain impossible. She was just preparing to turn her down gently when she spoke first.

“Yes,” Yae-hime nodded. “Because our strength difference is so large, the only way is for me to use my medical technique to assist you.”

Hearing this, Alicia swallowed back the refusal that had already risen to her lips. She knew better than anyone how extraordinary Yae-hime’s medical ability was. After all, she had dragged her back from the edge of death. Skill like that was nothing short of divine.

“And after the previous treatment, I may now understand your body even better than you do. Helping you restore your strength will not be an issue.” Yae-hime continued.

Alicia’s cheeks flushed at those words. Even though she had a special fondness toward Yae-hime… The thought of her body being thoroughly examined while she was unconscious was undeniably embarrassing.

“If everything’s fine, then let’s begin.” Yae-hime gently patted Lili’s head, and her small face also turned faintly red.

Lili disliked having her head touched, but whenever Yae-hime did it, she always felt surprisingly comfortable. Unfortunately, after a few strokes, Yae-hime withdrew her hand and lifted Lili down from her lap.

“O-okay. W-what do I need to do?” Alicia asked from the side, sounding slightly nervous.

“First, remove your clothes.” Yae-hime said calmly.

“Huh?” A shower of question marks practically popped above Alicia’s head.

Lili looked puzzled as well.

“I need to make direct contact with several areas of your body to properly guide the earth energy and wood energy into you.” Seeing their confusion, Yae-hime explained.

“I… I see.” Alicia only half-understood.

Lili nodded. She had seen Yae-hime’s treatment method earlier, and it indeed required the patient to be undressed. If clothing interfered and caused an error, that would be terrible.

“It’s getting late. Prepare yourself and we’ll start.” Yae-hime said. She still had to return to Aoma Village later to keep watch for the Apostle who might arrive.

‘I have four shards now. If I can get three more, I’ll be able to obtain a Sacred Artifact!’ It was a good plan in theory. Sadly, she didn’t know that the First Apostle had already shifted targets and was now focusing on the Sky Empire.

“I-I’ll undress now!” Alicia said, visibly tense. If one looked closely, they would see her body trembling slightly. She had been seen completely before, yes—but she had been unconscious for most of it, so she hadn’t felt particularly embarrassed. Now, undressing in front of Yae-hime while fully awake… the anxiety and shame were overwhelming.

As for being seen by her own sister Lili? Nothing strange about that. They had even bathed together as children.

Soft rustling filled the room as Alicia’s garments came off piece by piece. Meanwhile, her face grew hotter and hotter. Only after quite a struggle did she finally take everything off, becoming as bare as she had been earlier.

The difference was that now it was infinitely more humiliating. It felt like a public execution.

Yae-hime’s gaze showed no ripple at the sight of her beautiful figure. To be honest, her own body was more pleasing to the eye.

‘I’ll tidy Alicia’s physique up a little after this is over.’ A single glance revealed countless small flaws across Alicia’s body. For someone who trained in martial arts, having no imperfections would be the real anomaly.

“Come sit on the bed. I’ll guide you to absorb both earth energy and wood energy at the same time.” Yae-hime said as she removed her boots and sat cross-legged on the bed.

Alicia nodded. Her expression was stiff and unnatural. Her hands twitched as if she wanted to cover herself, but she couldn’t bring herself to act. Her entire body was frozen with embarrassment.

‘Hehe, Big Sis looks so adorable like this.’ Lili couldn’t help covering her mouth as she quietly giggled.

In response, Alicia shot her a small, slightly annoyed glance. She sat down on the bed and, just like Yae-hime, folded her legs into a cross-legged position. The two of them faced each other, their knees separated by only a fist’s distance.

“Relax. Steady your mind,” Yae-hime said.

“O-oh!” Alicia nodded vigorously, then took a deep breath to calm herself. After several seconds, she finally settled into a state of stillness, her mind becoming completely tranquil.

“Next, all you need to do is close your eyes, feel the flow of the energy in your body, and remember it. Don’t do anything else. When it’s time for you to act, I will tell you.” Yae-hime instructed.

“Alright.” Alicia replied, her expression steady.

Lili sat quietly on a chair nearby, silently watching the two of them.

“Before that, I’ll test manipulating the earth energy.” As she spoke, Yae-hime extended her hand, palm up. Her expression sharpened, and a surge of powerful aura burst forth from her entire body.

In the next moment, the entire mountain peak began to tremble!

Outside, Moon was startled by the sudden upheaval, but once she sensed the aura inside, she quickly composed herself. “For someone so young to possess such frightening potential… Princess’ growth is truly something to look forward to.” She murmured softly.

Inside the cave, both Lili and Alicia wore astonished expressions. First, they were shocked by how much stronger Yae-hime had grown. Then came the shock of the sheer volume of earth energy inside the cave. It was so dense it was almost suffocating!

Yae-hime gently curled her fingers, and the earth energy responded as if deeply captivated, sweeping toward her all at once.

‘Little Hime’s control over earth energy is completely different from Big Sis! She handles it as naturally as her own breath!’ Lili thought.

“No wonder she’s called the Child of Destiny,” Alicia murmured in admiration.

They were amazed, but Yae-hime was just as shocked in her own heart. ‘What’s going on? Am I… manipulating earth power?’ Suddenly, she remembered the new ability she had obtained earlier, Basic Earth Force.

‘So it really is earth manipulation… I hit the jackpot!’ In that moment, the earth energy draped itself over Yae-hime like a thin veil of gauze. It gave her an air both sacred and solemn.

Looking at her like this, a phrase surfaced instantly in Alicia’s mind: Child of Earth.

That was a title granted only to those favored by the Earth God. Clearly, someone who could freely manipulate the power of earth, like Yae-hime, was fully qualified for such a title. However, to Yae-hime herself, titles had little value. Money was far more practical.

“Calm yourself,” Yae-hime said, turning to Alicia with a serene gaze.

After a few seconds of adjustment, Alicia had already steadied herself completely. Hearing the instruction, she immediately closed her eyes and centered her mind. At that same moment, Yae-hime extended her other hand, and a verdant flame rose from her palm.

The wood energy contained within that green fire was countless times purer than the natural wood energy in this place. With both hands ready, Yae-hime’s pupils shifted into a brilliant emerald green as she peered directly into Alicia’s body.

Then, she placed one hand over Alicia’s chest and the other on her abdomen, sending two powerful flows of energy flooding into her simultaneously!
